<span class="akn-akomaNtoso"><article class="akn-act" data-contains="originalVersion" data-name="act"><section class="akn-preface" id="preface"><span class="akn-longTitle"><span class="akn-p">To regulate and control municipal zoning.</span></span><span class="akn-p">Under the provisions of section 156 of the <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1996/constitution" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1996/constitution">Constitution of the Republic of South Africa, 1996</a> the Bergrivier Municipality enacts as follows:</span></section><span class="akn-body"><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_1" data-eId="chp_1"><h2>Chapter 1<br>Interpretation</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_1" data-eId="sec_1"><h3>1. Definitions</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In this by-law, unless the context indicates otherwise, any word or expression to which a meaning has been assigned in the Western Cape <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Land_Use_Planning_Act" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_1">Land Use Planning Act</span>, 2014 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/2014/3" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/2014/3">Act 3 of 2014</a>) has the meaning assigned to it in that Act and</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-ancillary">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-ancillary">ancillary</span>" means a land use, purpose, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_2">building</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-structure" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_3">structure</span> or activity which is directly related to, and subservient to, the lawful <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dominant_use" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_4">dominant use</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_5">property</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-antenna">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-antenna">antenna</span>" means any system of wires, poles, rods, reflective surfaces or similar devices, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-used" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_6">used</span> to transmit or receive electronic communication signals or electro-magnetic waves;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-applicant">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-applicant">applicant</span>" means a person who makes application in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Planning_By_law" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_7">Planning By-law</span>;</span><span class="akn-blockList" data-refersTo="#term-atrium" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-atrium">atrium</span> means a covered courtyard that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">comprises a void within a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">building</span> that extends for one or more floors in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">height</span> which contains a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-floor" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_3">floor</span> and roof or ceiling; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">does not contain floors that penetrate into the void;</span></span></span><span class="akn-blockList" data-refersTo="#term-average_ground_level" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-average_ground_level">average ground level</span>" means the average of the highest and lowest existing ground levels immediately abutting the external elevational plane or wall cutting into the ground of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__term_1">building</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vertical_division" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__term_2">vertical division</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__term_3">building</span>, and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__term_4">Municipality</span> may:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_a" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">determine the average ground level from measurements supplied on a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_a__term_1">building</span> plan; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_b" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">deem a level to be the average ground level based on measurements interpolated from a contour plan, local <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_b__term_1">height</span> benchmark or other information held by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_b__term_2">Municipality</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_c" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">require the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_c__term_1">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_c__term_2">applicant</span> to commission a registered surveyor to measure levels of the ground or interpolate levels, in order to provide         the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_2__item_c__term_3">Municipality</span> with sufficient information so that it can determine the average ground level for the purpose of administering this By-law;</span></span></span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-balcony">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-balcony">balcony</span>" means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-floor" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_8" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_8">floor</span> projecting outside a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_9" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_9">building</span> at a level higher than that of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-ground_floor" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_10" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_10">ground floor</span>, enclosed only by low walls or railings or by containing walls of rooms abutting the projecting <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-floor" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_11" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_11">floor</span>, and may include a roof over the projecting <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-floor" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_12" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_12">floor</span> and pillars supporting the roof;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-base_level">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-base_level">base level</span>" of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_13" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_13">building</span> means an imaginary plane drawn horizontally at the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-average_ground_level" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_14" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_14">average ground level</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_15" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_15">building</span>, or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-vertical_division" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_16" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_16">vertical division</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_17" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_17">building</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-base_zone">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-base_zone">base zone</span>" means that zone which determines the lawful land use and development parameters for a land unit in terms of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_18" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_18">zoning</span> scheme, before the application of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-overlay_zone" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_19" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_6__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_6__item_c__term_1">building</span> or <span class="akn-term" demolished;</span></span></span><span class="akn-blockList" data-refersTo="#term-existing_ground_level" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-existing_ground_level">existing ground level</span>" means the level of the land surface on a land unit:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_a" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">in its unmodified state, before any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_a__term_1">building</span> had been erected or alterations in levels had been made thereon; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_b" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">as established from a plan indicating the contours of the land lodged with and accepted by an official agency such as the municipality or a          government department, which depicts the existing level of the ground at or before the commencement date; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_c" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">in a state which has been graded, with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_c__term_1">Municipality</span>s approval, for the purpose of development; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_d" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_d__term_1">Municipality</span>, if in its opinion it is not possible to ascertain the existing level of the ground due to irregularities          or disturbances of the land; and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_d__term_2">Municipality</span> may require the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_d__term_3" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_d__term_3">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_d__term_4" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_d__term_4">applicant</span> to commission a registered surveyor to measure levels of         the ground or interpolate levels, which shall be tied to the National Control Network, or where this is not possible, to provide at least two         durable reference marks suitably located, in order to provide the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_d__term_5" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_7__item_d__term_5">Municipality</span> with sufficient information so that it can determine the most         appropriate existing ground level for the purpose of administrating this By-law;</span></span></span><span class="akn-blockList" data-refersTo="#term-family" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-family">family</span>" means</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_a" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">one or more individuals occupying a dwelling who are related through marriage or common law, blood relationship, legal adoption, or legal            guardianship and unrelated domestic workers and boarders; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_b" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a group of not more than 5 unrelated persons including domestic workers or boarders;</span></span></span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-flood_prone_area">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-flood_prone_area">flood-prone area</span>" means any land area susceptible to being inundated by water from any source;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-floor">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-floor">floor</span>" means the inner, lower surface of a room, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-garage" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_61" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_61">garage</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-basement" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_62" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_62">basement</span>, and includes a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-terrace" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_63" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_63">terrace</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-atrium" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_64" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_64">atrium</span> to which the occupants of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_65" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_65">building</span> have access;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-floor_factor">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-floor_factor">floor factor</span>" means the factor, expressed as a proportion of 1, which is prescribed for the calculation of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-maximum_floor_space" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_66" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_66">maximum floor space</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_67" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_67">building</span> or buildings permissible on a land unit. If the floor factor is known, the maximum permissible <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-floor_space" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_68" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_68">floor space</span> can be calculated by multiplying the floor factor by the area of the land unit;</span><span class="akn-p">Maximum <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-floor_space" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_69" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_69">floor space</span> = (Floor factor)  (Area of the land unit)</span><span class="akn-blockList" data-refersTo="#term-floor_space" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-floor_space">floor space</span>", in relation to any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__term_1">building</span>, means the area of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-floor" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__term_2">floor</span> which is covered by a slab, roof or projection; provided that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-basement" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a__term_1">basement</span> or part of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-basement" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a__term_2">basement</span> not intended as habitable space shall be excluded;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_b" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">any area which is reserved solely for parking or loading of vehicles shall be excluded;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_c" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">external <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-entrance_steps_and_landings" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_c__term_1">entrance steps and landings</span>, a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-canopy" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_c__term_2">canopy</span>, a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-stoep" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_c__term_3">stoep</span> and an area required for external fire escapes are excluded;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_d" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">a projection, including a projection of eaves, and a projection which acts as a sunscreen or an architectural feature, which projection does         not exceed 1 metre beyond the exterior wall or similar support, is excluded;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_e" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">any uncovered internal courtyard, light well or other uncovered shaft which has an area in excess of 10 m is excluded;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_f" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">any covered paved area outside and immediately adjoining a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_f__term_1">building</span> at or below the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-ground_floor" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_f__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_f__term_2">ground floor</span> level, where such paved area is part of a           forecourt, yard, external courtyard, pedestrian walkway, parking area or vehicular access, and which is permanently open to the elements on          at least the front or long side, is excluded;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_g" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">any covered <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-balcony" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_g__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_g__term_1">balcony</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-verandah" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_g__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_g__term_2">verandah</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-terrace" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_g__term_3" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_g__term_3">terrace</span> which, apart from protective railings, is permanently open to the elements on at least the front or         long side, and which does not exceed 2,5 metres in width, is excluded;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_h" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">subject to paragraph (i), any stairs, stairwells and atriums that are covered by a roof are included;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i__list_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">in the case of multi-level buildings, any stairwells, lift wells, light wells or other wells, and any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-atrium" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i__list_1__term_1">atrium</span>, are only counted once; and             provided further that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">floor space is measured from the outer face of the exterior walls or similar supports of the multi-level <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i__list_1__item_i__term_1">building</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-total_floor_space" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i__list_1__item_ii__term_1">total floor space</span> is the sum of the floor space of all the levels of the multi-level <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i__list_1__item_ii__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i__list_1__item_ii__term_2">building</span>, including that of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-basement" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i__list_1__item_ii__term_3" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_i__list_1__item_ii__term_3">basement</span>;</span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-garage">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-garage">garage</span>" means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_70" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_70">building</span> for the storage of one or more motor vehicles, and includes a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-carport" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_71" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_71">carport</span> but does not include a motor repair garage or service station;</span><span class="akn-blockList" data-refersTo="#term-GLA" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-GLA">GLA</span>" means gross leasable area being the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-total_floor_space" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__term_1">total floor space</span> designed for, or capable of, occupancy or control by tenants, measured from the centre line of the joint partitions to the inside finished surface of the outside walls, but excludes public toilets, internal walkways, lift shafts, service ducts, interior parking and loading bays and shall exclude the following:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_a" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">areas reasonably <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-used" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_a__term_1">used</span> in connection with the cleaning, maintenance and care of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_a__term_2">building</span>, excluding dwelling units for caretakers,                supervisors, cleaners or maintenance staff;</span></span></span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-greenhouse">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-greenhouse">greenhouse</span>" means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-structure" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_72" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_72">structure</span> with the sides primarily made of a transparent material such as glass, perspex or plastic for the purpose of growing of plants or hastening growth of plants under controlled environmental conditions;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-ground_floor">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-ground_floor">ground floor</span>" means the lowest <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-floor" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_73" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_73">floor</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_74" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_74">building</span> that is not a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-basement" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_75" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_75">basement</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-gross_density">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-gross_density">gross density</span>" means a measure of the number of dwelling units in a specified area, and is calculated as follows:</span><span class="akn-p">Gross dwelling density (units per hectare) = Total number of dwelling units in a specified area / Extent of specified area in hectares;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-hazardous_substance">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-hazardous_substance">hazardous substance</span>" has the same meaning as grouped hazardous substance as defined in section 1 of the Hazardous Substances Act, 1973           (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1973/15" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1973/15">Act 15 of 1973</a>);</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-height">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-height">height</span>" of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_76" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_76">building</span> means a vertical dimension from a specified level to another specified level, as set out in the development rules of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_77" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_77">zoning</span>/land use category, measured in metres; provided that chimneys (maximum horizontal dimension of 1.5m), flues (maximum horizontal dimension of 1m), lift shafts (maximum horizontal dimension of 2.5; maximum vertical dimension of 3m), masts and antennas shall not be counted for the purposes of height control;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-kitchen">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-kitchen">kitchen</span>" means a room or part of a room equipped for preparing and cooking meals and excludes a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-braai_room" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_78" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_78">braai room</span>, food and drink preparation area or bar facilities in an entertainment area;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Land_Use_Planning_Act">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Land_Use_Planning_Act">Land Use Planning Act</span>" means the Western Cape Land Use Planning Act, 2014 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/2014/3" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/2014/3">Act 3 of 2014</a>);</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-landscaping">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-landscaping">landscaping</span>" means the placement of plants, contoured features, water features, paving, street furniture and other soft and hard elements for the purposes of enhancing the aesthetic appeal, environmental management, amenity and value of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_79" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_79">property</span> or area;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-loading_bay">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-loading_bay">loading bay</span>" means an area which is clearly demarcated for the loading and off-loading of goods from <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-commercial" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_80" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_80">commercial</span> vehicles, and which has vehicular access to a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_street" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_81" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_81">public street</span> to the satisfaction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_82" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_82">Municipality</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-lodger">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-lodger">lodger</span>" means a person who utilises <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-lodging" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_83" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_83">lodging</span> services;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-lodging">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-lodging">lodging</span>" means the provision of bedroom accommodation or, in the case of a backpackers lodge, bed accommodation that is made available on payment of a charge or fee, and includes the services ordinarily related to such accommodation;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-maximum_floor_space">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-maximum_floor_space">maximum floor space</span>" means the greatest <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-total_floor_space" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_84" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_84">total floor space</span> that is allowed for a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_85" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_85">building</span> or buildings on a land unit, and is calculated by multiplying the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-floor_factor" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_86" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_86">floor factor</span> by the area of the land unit or that portion of the land unit which is situated within a particular zone; provided that, where the land unit is situated within two or more zones to which different <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-floor" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_87" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_87">floor</span> factors apply, the maximum floor space for the whole land unit is the total of the maximum floor space for each zoned portion of the land unit;</span><span class="akn-blockList" data-refersTo="#term-mineral" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-mineral">mineral</span>" means a substance, whether in solid, liquid or gaseous form, occurring naturally in or on the earth or under water and which was formed by or subjected to a geological process, and includes sand, stone, rock, gravel, clay, soil and any material occurring in residue stockpiles or in residue deposits, but excludes</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_a" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">water, other than water taken from land or sea for the extraction of any mineral from such water; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_b" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">petroleum.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-motor_vehicle">"<span any employee of the Municipality acting in terms of delegated or sub-delegated authority of the Municipality;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-National_Building_Regulations">"<span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-natural_ground_level">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-natural_ground_level">natural ground level</span>" see '<span class="akn-term" by-laws governing occupational health and safety, whichever is applicable;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-outbuilding">"<span class="akn-def" Environmental Management Act, 1998 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1998/107" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1998/107">Act 107 of 1998</a>))</span></span></span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-youth_hostel">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-youth_hostel">youth hostel</span>" means a place providing cheap accommodation, aimed mainly at young tourists;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-zoning">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-zoning">zoning</span>" includes base zoning and overlay zoning;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-zoning_scheme_of_the_Municipality">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-zoning_scheme_of_the_Municipality">zoning scheme of the Municipality</span>" means the components referred to in section 4 adopted by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_192" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_192">Municipality</span> for the regulation of land use.</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_2" data-eId="chp_2"><h2>Chapter 2<br>Zoning scheme, use zones and uses</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_2" data-eId="sec_2"><h3>2. Application of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__term_1">zoning</span> scheme</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_2__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_2__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_1">zoning</span> scheme applies to the entire municipal area.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_3" data-eId="sec_3"><h3>3. Purpose of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__term_1">zoning</span> scheme</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The purpose of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">zoning</span> scheme is to</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">enable the municipal <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-spatial_development_framework" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">spatial development framework</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">make provision for orderly development and the welfare of the community; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">determine use rights and development parameters, with due consideration of the principles referred to in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Land_Use_Planning_Act" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">Land Use Planning Act</span>.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_4" data-eId="sec_4"><h3>4. Components of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__term_1">zoning</span> scheme</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_4__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_4__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_4__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_4__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_4__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">zoning</span> scheme consists of the following components:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_4__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">this by-law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_4__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_4__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">zoning</span> scheme map; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_4__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the register.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_5" data-eId="sec_5"><h3>5. Use zones</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_5__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The municipal area is divided in the use zones referred to in column 1 of the table set out in Schedule 1.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_5__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The purpose of each use zone is set out in column 1 of the table set out in Schedule 1.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_5__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The description of the primary and consent uses applicable to each use zone is set out in Schedule 2.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_5__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The location, boundaries and extent of each use zone is depicted on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_5__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_4__term_1">zoning</span> scheme map.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_5__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The primary and consent uses applicable to each use zone are subject to the development parameters specified for that use zone as set out in Schedule 2.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_6" data-eId="sec_6"><h3>6. Zoning scheme map</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">zoning</span> scheme map depicts</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">zoning</span> of land in accordance with the use zone in which the land is located; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">overlay zones, if applicable to the land.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_6__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span> must update the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_6__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2__term_2">zoning</span> scheme map within a reasonable time after use rights have been granted or have lapsed.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_6__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> may keep the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_6__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_3__term_2">zoning</span> scheme map in an electronic format.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_6__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_4__term_1">Municipality</span> may provide an extract of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_6__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_4__term_2">zoning</span> map to members of the public on payment of a fee determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_6__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_4__term_3">Municipality</span> in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_6__subsec_4__term_4" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_4__term_4">Municipality</span>s tariff policy.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_7" data-eId="sec_7"><h3>7. Transition to new use zones and savings</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Upon the effective date of this By-law, land that is zoned in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-previous_zoning_regulations" id="sec_7__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1__term_1">previous zoning regulations</span> is translated or reclassified to one of the use zones referred to in section 5.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Translation or reclassification of the use zones <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-used" id="sec_7__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_2__term_1">used</span> in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-previous_zoning_regulations" id="sec_7__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_2__term_2">previous zoning regulations</span> to the use zones <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-used" id="sec_7__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_2__term_3">used</span> in this By-law was done primarily by determining the closest match for each corresponding use zone. In individual cases where existing land use or other characteristics rendered the aforementioned match not suitable, individual assessments were undertaken to determine the appropriate new use zone.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Despite the translation or reclassification of the use zones <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-used" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">used</span> in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-previous_zoning_regulations" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__term_2">previous zoning regulations</span> to the use zones <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-used" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__term_3">used</span> in this By-law</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">any condition of approval or validity period that is applicable to a land unit in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-previous_zoning_regulations" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">previous zoning regulations</span> immediately before         the coming into effect of this By-law, remain applicable and is incorporated into this By-law in so far as it determines development rules or         restrictions that are different from the development rules or restrictions applicable in terms of this By-law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">Municipality</span> must record any development rule, condition and parameter referred to in paragraph (a) together with any applicable validity         period applicable to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2">zoning</span> in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-previous_zoning_regulations" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_3">previous zoning regulations</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1">zoning</span> that has been exercised prior to coming into effect of this By-law, cannot lapse, and is translated or reclassified as determined in         this By-law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_1">zoning</span> approved in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-previous_zoning_regulations" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_2">previous zoning regulations</span> that has not been exercised immediately before the coming into effect of this          By-law, lapses after the expiry of the validity period applicable to that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_3">zoning</span> in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-previous_zoning_regulations" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_4" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_4">previous zoning regulations</span> and is                  translated or reclassified as determined in this By-law; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">in the event of the lapsing of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_1">zoning</span> as contemplated in paragraph (d), the land unit reverts back to the use zone applicable to it in             terms of the previous regulations, before it was rezoned and is translated or reclassified as outlined in subsection (2).</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_8" data-eId="sec_8"><h3>8. Rectification of errors on <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_8__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__term_1">zoning</span> scheme map</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_8__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1__term_1">zoning</span> of a land unit is incorrectly indicated on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_8__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1__term_2">zoning</span> map, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_8__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1__term_3">owner</span> of an affected land unit may submit an application to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1__term_4">Municipality</span> to correct the error.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_8__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_8__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">owner</span> contemplated in subsection (1) must apply to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">Municipality</span> in the form determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_2__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__list_1__term_3">Municipality</span> and must</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_8__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">submit written proof of the lawful land use rights; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_8__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">indicate the suitable <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_8__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">zoning</span> which should be allocated.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The onus of proving that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_8__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__term_1">zoning</span> is incorrectly indicated on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_8__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__term_2">zoning</span> scheme map is on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_8__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__term_3">owner</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_8__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_4__term_1">owner</span> is exempted from paying application fees and from liability for the costs of public participation.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_8__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_5__term_1">zoning</span> of a land unit is incorrectly indicated on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_8__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_5__term_2">zoning</span> map, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_5__term_3">Municipality</span> must record the correct <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_8__subsec_5__term_4" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_5__term_4">zoning</span> on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_8__subsec_5__term_5" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_5__term_5">zoning</span> map.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the correct <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_8__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_6__term_1">zoning</span> of a land unit cannot be ascertained from the information submitted to theMunicipality or the records of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_6__term_2">Municipality</span>, a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_8__subsec_6__term_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_6__term_3">zoning</span> determination in terms of the By-law on Municipal Land Use Planning should be processed and the outcome of such determination must be recorded on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_8__subsec_6__term_4" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_6__term_4">zoning</span> scheme map.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_9" data-eId="sec_9"><h3>9. Zoning scheme register</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_9__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_9__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_9__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_9__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">must record all departures, consent uses or other permissions granted and non-conforming uses in the register;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_9__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">may keep the register from the date of commencement of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_9__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">zoning</span> scheme in an electronic format; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_9__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">must make the register available to members of the public for viewing.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_10" data-eId="sec_10"><h3>10. Primary uses</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_10__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_10__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Primary uses of land permitted in each use zone, without the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_10__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__hcontainer_1__term_1">Municipality</span>s consent, are listed in the corresponding part of column 2 of the table set out in Schedule 1.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_11" data-eId="sec_11"><h3>11. Consent uses</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_11__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_11__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Consent uses of land permitted in each use zone, with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_11__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__hcontainer_1__term_1">Municipality</span>s prior consent in terms of its <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Planning_By_law" id="sec_11__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__hcontainer_1__term_2">Planning By-law</span>, is listed in the corresponding part of column 3 of the table set out in Schedule 1.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_12" data-eId="sec_12"><h3>12. Occasional uses</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_12__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_12__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> must record the relevant information relating to occasional uses applicable to a land unit in the register.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_12__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Approval of a use right as an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occasional_use" id="sec_12__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_2__term_1">occasional use</span> in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Planning_By_law" id="sec_12__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_12__subsec_2__term_2">Planning By-law</span> must at least be subject to the development parameters applicable to the use right as stipulated in this by-law.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_13" data-eId="sec_13"><h3>13. Non-conforming uses</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-non_conforming_use" id="sec_13__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__term_1">non-conforming use</span> does not constitute an offence in terms of this by-law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-non_conforming_use" id="sec_13__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_2__term_1">non-conforming use</span> may continue as long as it remains otherwise lawful.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_14" data-eId="sec_14"><h3>14. Deemed <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_14__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__term_1">zoning</span> of closed public places</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">zoning</span> of land that was previously a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_street" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2">public street</span> or public open space, vested in or owned by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_3">Municipality</span> and that is closed, is determined as follows:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">if the land is transferred to an abutting land <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">owner</span>, that portion of the land falls in the same zone as that of the abutting land belonging         to the abutting <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">owner</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> must determine which <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_2">zoning</span> applies to the land if</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the land is transferred to an abutting land <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1">owner</span> and that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_2" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_2">owner</span> owns abutting properties falling into more than one zone; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">in any other case not provided for in this section.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_3" data-eId="chp_3"><h2>Chapter 3<br>Overlay zones</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_15" data-eId="sec_15"><h3>15. Purpose of overlay zones</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may adopt, review or amend overlay zones for specific areas in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">Municipality</span> in accordance with the procedures stipulated in section 19 to</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">give expression, in a planning context, to the local needs and values of the communities concerned; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">promote particular types of development, urban form, landscape character, environmental features or heritage values.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span> must determine development parameters for each area of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-overlay_zone" id="sec_15__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__term_2">overlay zone</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_16" data-eId="sec_16"><h3>16. Procedures for establishing, reviewing or amending overlay zones</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_16__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_16__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-overlay_zone" id="sec_16__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_16__hcontainer_1__term_1">overlay zone</span> is adopted, reviewed or amended by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_16__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_16__hcontainer_1__term_2">Municipality</span> as an amendment of this by-law in accordance with sections 12 and 13 of the Municipal Systems Act, 2000 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/2000/32" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/2000/32">Act 32 of 2000</a>) and section 25 of the Land Use Planning Act.</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_4" data-eId="chp_4"><h2>Chapter 4<br>Distances, heights, levels and boundaries</h2>
<h3 class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_4__hcontainer_1" data-eId="chp_4__hcontainer_1">Measuring distances, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="chp_4__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_4__hcontainer_1__term_1">height</span> and levels</h3>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_17" data-eId="sec_17"><h3>17. Methods of measuring distances, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_17__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__term_1">height</span> and levels</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following provisions apply with regard to measuring distances, levels or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">height</span>:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">If required by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">Municipality</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">owner</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_3">applicant</span> shall appoint a registered surveyor to supply or verify information necessary for the         <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_4" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_4">Municipality</span> to make a decision about compliance with distances or levels required in terms of this by-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Where reference is made or implied to the distance between boundaries or between a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1">building</span> and a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_2">boundary</span>, this distance shall be measured          in the following manner:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1">boundary</span> or boundaries and all points of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_2">building</span> shall be projected onto a horizontal plane, and all measurements shall be made             on such a plane; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">The distance between a point on a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1">building</span> and a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_2">boundary</span> shall be measured at the shortest distance between the point and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_3" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_3">boundary</span>.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">Where reference is made to a portion of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">boundary</span> opposite a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">building</span>, such portion shall be defined by drawing lines in the manner               described in paragraph (b) from points on such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_3">building</span>, at right angles to such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_4" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_4">boundary</span>.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">Any post-construction deviation from a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">height</span> restriction that does not exceed 300 mm will not be considered a contravention of the                  provisions of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_2">zoning</span> scheme, provided that this deviation provision does not apply for the purposes of making an application.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If there is doubt about the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_1">height</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_2">building</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-structure" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_3">structure</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_4">Municipality</span> may require the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_5">owner</span> to appoint a registered surveyor to:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">certify the actual <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i__term_1">height</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i__term_2">building</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-structure" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i__term_3" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i__term_3">structure</span> in accordance with the provisions of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i__term_4" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i__term_4">zoning</span> scheme;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">certify if a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii__term_1">building</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-structure" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii__term_2">structure</span> is in contravention of the provisions of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii__term_3" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii__term_3">zoning</span> scheme; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">certify that all structures on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii__term_1">property</span> comply with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii__term_2">height</span> restrictions applicable to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii__term_3" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii__term_3">property</span>.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">Where reference is made to a distance, ground level, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_1">height</span> of a point on a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_2">building</span> or other measurement, then such distance, level or              <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_3" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_3">height</span> shall be calculated in accordance with recognised geometric principles, and for the purposes of determining contours, from any data           set held by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_4" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_4">Municipality</span> at or before the commencement date or any data set so determined by the <span class="akn-term"
