data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_5" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_5">Municipality</span>. In any case where the             distance, level or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_6" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_6">height</span> involved is so irregular that calculation in accordance with these principles is impractical or leads to a result          which is clearly not in accordance with the intent of the By-law, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_7" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_7">Municipality</span> shall determine the distance, level or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_8" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_8">height</span> concerned           for the purpose of administering this By-law.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_18" data-eId="sec_18"><h3>18. Determining boundaries of use zones</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If uncertainty exists as to the boundaries of use zones, the following parameters apply in the order listed:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">boundaries shown as following or approximately following any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_street" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">public street</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-road" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">road</span> must be construed as following the street cadastral               <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_3">boundary</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">boundaries shown as following or approximately following any land unit <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">boundary</span> must be construed as following that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">boundary</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">boundaries shown as following or approximately following natural features must be construed as following those features; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">in the event of further uncertainty as to the boundaries of a use zone, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">Municipality</span> must make a determination.</span></span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_5" data-eId="chp_5"><h2>Chapter 5<br>Enforcement</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_19" data-eId="sec_19"><h3>19. Offences, penalties and enforcement of this by-law</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Subject to section 19, no person may erect any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">building</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-structure" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">structure</span> or any part thereof</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">except for a purpose permitted by this by-law and only in accordance with the applicable development parameters; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">without first obtaining approval from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">Municipality</span> in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Planning_By_law" id="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">Planning By-law</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A use not reflected as a primary or consent use for a particular use zone is not permitted in the use zone concerned, unless approved in terms of the Planning By-Law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> must enforce the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_19__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_3__term_2">zoning</span> scheme through the measures for enforcement provided for in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Planning_By_law" id="sec_19__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_3__term_3">Planning By-law</span>.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_6" data-eId="chp_6"><h2>Chapter 6<br>Development of land</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_20" data-eId="sec_20"><h3>20. Development parameters applicable to use rights</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The land use descriptions and development parameters applicable to each primary and consent use right depicted in the table in Schedule 1 are described in Schedule 2.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Development parameters are applicable to use rights only and, notwithstanding the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_20__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__term_1">zoning</span> of an erf, a specific use right will always have the same development parameters as listed in Schedule 2, provided that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__term_2">Municipality</span> may grant a departure from the development parameters in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Planning_By_law" id="sec_20__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__term_3">Planning By-law</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_20__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Consent uses, as listed in Column 3 of Schedule 1, shall be subject to the following conditions:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_20__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">when a consent use is granted in a particular zone, the applicable land use must be supplementary to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-primary_use" id="sec_20__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">primary use</span> right allowed under the         particular zone; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_20__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">when it is intended to utilise land exclusively for a consent use in a particular zone which is a primary right in another zone, application         must be made for rezoning to the zone where the applicable land use is a primary right.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No departure from the land use descriptions or definitions may be granted.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding subsections (1) and (2), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_5__term_1">Municipality</span> may determine additional conditions with regard to any specific <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_20__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_5__term_2">property</span> which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_5__term_3">Municipality</span> may lawfully do in terms of relevant legislation.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_7" data-eId="chp_7"><h2>Chapter 7<br>General provisions</h2>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="chp_7__hcontainer_1" data-eId="chp_7__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">This part contains general provisions and parameters that apply to all zones or to specific zones as may be provided for. It includes matters such as encroachments that may occur within <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="chp_7__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_7__hcontainer_1__term_1">building</span> lines and requirements for site development plans. It refers to hazardous substances, owners      associations, screening, retaining structures, outdoor storage, antennae systems and other municipal by-laws. This part also contains requirements for parking, loading, access and infrastructure. There are also provisions relating to the subdivision of land.</span></span></span><section class="akn-section" id="sec_21" data-eId="sec_21"><h3>21. Encroachment of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_21__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__term_1">building</span> lines</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_21__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Notwithstanding the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building_line" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">building line</span> requirements set out in Chapter 6, the following structures or portions of structures may be erected within the prescribed <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">building</span> lines, provided they do not extend beyond the boundaries of a land unit:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">boundary</span> walls, fences and gates;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">open and uncovered stoeps that are less than 500 millimetres in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">height</span> from the natural level of the ground;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">entrance steps, landings and entrance porches, excluding porte cochres;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">a covered entrance or gatehouse that has a roofed area not exceeding 5 m and a roof <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">height</span> not exceeding 3 metres from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-floor" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2">floor</span> to the             highest point;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">eaves and awnings projecting no more than 1 metre from the wall of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1">building</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">cornices, chimney breasts, flower boxes, water pipes, drain pipes and minor decorative features not projecting more than 500 millimetres from         the wall of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1">building</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">screen-walls not exceeding 2,1 metres in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_1">height</span> above the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-natural_ground_level" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_2">natural ground level</span> abutting such wall;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">swimming pools not closer than 1 metre from any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_h__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_h__term_1">boundary</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-basement" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__term_1">basement</span>, provided that no part of such a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-basement" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__term_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__term_2">basement</span> projects above <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-natural_ground_level" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__term_3" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__term_3">natural ground level</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_j" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-refuse_room" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_j__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_j__term_1">refuse room</span> required by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_j__term_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__list_1__item_j__term_2">Municipality</span> in terms of this by-law.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_21__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">For the purposes of determining street boundaries a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-street_centreline_setback" id="sec_21__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_2__term_1">street centreline setback</span> and site access requirements the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_21__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_2__term_2">boundary</span> of a pedestrian way or service lane that cannot or will never be <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-used" id="sec_21__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_2__term_3">used</span> by motor vehicles may be regarded as a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-common_boundary" id="sec_21__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_2__term_4">common boundary</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_21__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No application for departure of a side <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building_line" id="sec_21__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__term_1">building line</span> is required if the abutting neighbour gives written consent for the encroachment of the relevant <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building_line" id="sec_21__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__term_2">building line</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_22" data-eId="sec_22"><h3>22. Street centreline setback</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_22__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_22__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The portion of a land unit falling within a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-street_centreline_setback" id="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_1">street centreline setback</span> area is excluded for the purpose of determining <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-coverage" id="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_2">coverage</span> and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-maximum_floor_space" id="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_3">maximum floor space</span>, unless the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_4">owner</span> transfers the portion concerned to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_5">Municipality</span> free of charge. In such case, the portion must be included for the purpose of determining <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-coverage" id="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_6">coverage</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-maximum_floor_space" id="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_7">maximum floor space</span> on a land unit.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_23" data-eId="sec_23"><h3>23. Site development plans</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">In addition to the zones that specifically require a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-site_development_plan" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">site development plan</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">Municipality</span> may require a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-site_development_plan" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">site development plan</span> in respect of the following development types:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">shopping centres and shopping complexes;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">business and office park developments;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">industrial park developments;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">developments in conservation areas;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">developments that will be sectionalised;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">incremental residential developments;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">major developments where there are concerns relating to urban form, heritage, traffic or planning; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">any other development type that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_h__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__list_1__item_h__term_1">Municipality</span> may deem applicable/relevant.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may require some or all of the following information for a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-site_development_plan" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">site development plan</span>-</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">existing bio-physical characteristics of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">property</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">existing and proposed cadastral boundaries;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the layout of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">property</span>, indicating the use of different portions of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2">property</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the massing, position, use and extent of buildings;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">sketch plans and elevations of proposed structures, including information about their external appearance;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">cross-sections of the site and buildings on site;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">the alignment and general specification of vehicle access, roads, parking areas, loading areas, pedestrian flow and footpaths;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">any measures of access control to and reservation of parking spaces/areas;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the position and extent of private, public and communal space;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_j" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">typical details of fencing or walls around the perimeter of the land unit and within the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_j__term_1">property</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_k" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">electricity supply and external lighting proposals;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_l" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_l"><span class="akn-num">(l)</span><span class="akn-p">provisions for the supply of water, management of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-storm_water" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_l__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_l__term_1">storm water</span>, and disposal of sewage and refuse;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_m" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_m"><span class="akn-num">(m)</span><span class="akn-p">external signage details;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_n" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_n"><span class="akn-num">(n)</span><span class="akn-p">general <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-landscaping" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_n__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_n__term_1">landscaping</span> proposals, including vegetation to be preserved, removed or to be planted, external paving, and measures for stabilising         outdoor areas where applicable;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_o" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_o"><span class="akn-num">(o)</span><span class="akn-p">the phasing of a development;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_p" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_p"><span class="akn-num">(p)</span><span class="akn-p">the proposed development in relation to existing and finished ground levels, including excavation, cut and fill;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_q" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_q"><span class="akn-num">(q)</span><span class="akn-p">statistical information about the extent of the proposed development, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-floor" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_q__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_q__term_1">floor</span> area allocations and parking supply;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_r" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_r"><span class="akn-num">(r)</span><span class="akn-p">relationship of the proposed development to the quality, safety and amenity of the surrounding public environment;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_s" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_s"><span class="akn-num">(s)</span><span class="akn-p">relationship of the proposed development to adjacent sites, especially with respect to access, overshadowing and scale;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_t" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_t"><span class="akn-num">(t)</span><span class="akn-p">illustrations in a three-dimensional form depicting visual impacts of the proposed development on the site and in relation to surrounding            buildings; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_u" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_u"><span class="akn-num">(u)</span><span class="akn-p">any other details as may reasonably be required by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_u__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2__list_1__item_u__term_1">Municipality</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> may require that the area covered by a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-site_development_plan" id="sec_23__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__term_2">site development plan</span> must extend beyond the site under consideration if, in its opinion, the proposed development will have a wide impact.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_4__term_1">Municipality</span> may determine the extent of the area covered by a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-site_development_plan" id="sec_23__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_4__term_2">site development plan</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_23__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_5__term_1">applicant</span> must submit a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-site_development_plan" id="sec_23__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_5__term_2">site development plan</span> to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_5__term_3">Municipality</span> if it is required in terms of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_23__subsec_5__term_4" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_5__term_4">zoning</span> scheme before any development on the relevant land unit may commence.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_6__term_1">Municipality</span> may require amendments of detail to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-site_development_plan" id="sec_23__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_6__term_2">site development plan</span> to address reasonable concerns relating to access, parking, architectural form, urban form, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-landscaping" id="sec_23__subsec_6__term_3" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_6__term_3">landscaping</span>, environmental management, engineering services or similar concerns.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following provisions apply with regard to site development plans:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_a__term_1">property</span> must be developed generally in accordance with an approved <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-site_development_plan" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_a__term_2">site development plan</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_b__term_1">Municipality</span> considers it necessary, a transport or traffic impact statement or assessment may be required in conjunction with a site         development plan, the extent of which must be determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_b__term_2">Municipality</span>, depending on the size of the development;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_c__term_1">Municipality</span> considers it necessary, a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-storm_water" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_c__term_2">storm water</span> impact assessment or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-storm_water" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_c__term_3">storm water</span> management plan or both may be required in                conjunction with a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-site_development_plan" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_c__term_4" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_c__term_4">site development plan</span>, the extent of which must be determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_c__term_5" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_c__term_5">Municipality</span>, depending on the size of the                   development;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_d__term_1">Municipality</span> considers it necessary, a visual impact assessment, which may include a landscape character analysis, may be required in         conjunction with a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-site_development_plan" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_d__term_2">site development plan</span>, the extent of which must be determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_d__term_3" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_d__term_3">Municipality</span>, depending on the size of the                   development; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">an approved <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-site_development_plan" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_e__term_1">site development plan</span> must be considered as setting additional development parameters applicable to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-base_zone" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_e__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_e__term_2">base zone</span>, and any               application for amendment must comply with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_e__term_3" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_7__list_1__item_e__term_3">Municipality</span>s requirements for the amendments.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_24" data-eId="sec_24"><h3>24. Hazardous substances</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_24__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any use or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-ancillary" id="sec_24__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__term_1">ancillary</span> activity that involves the storage or keeping of hazardous substances that may result in an installation being declared a major hazardous installation in terms of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupational_health_and_safety_law" id="sec_24__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__term_2">occupational health and safety law</span> is not permitted, unless the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_24__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__term_3">owner</span> has submitted a risk management and prevention plan and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_24__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__term_4">Municipality</span> has given its approval to the plan.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_24__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_24__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span>s approval in terms of subsection (1) above does not exempt the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_24__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_2__term_2">owner</span> from applying for permission in terms of other relevant legislation.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_25" data-eId="sec_25"><h3>25. Screening</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_25__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_25__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_25__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_25__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_25__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may require screening in accordance with the following provisions:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_25__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">any part of a land unit which is <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-used" id="sec_25__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">used</span> for the storage or loading of goods must be enclosed with a suitable wall or landscape screening or            both; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_25__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">any external utility service or equipment which is required for a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_25__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">building</span> must be appropriately screened from view from a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_street" id="sec_25__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_25__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">public street</span>, and         the screening must be integrated with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_25__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_25__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_3">building</span> in terms of materials, colour, shape and size.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_26" data-eId="sec_26"><h3>26. Earth banks and retaining structures</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Unless the prior approval of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> has been obtained</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">no <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-earth_bank" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">earth bank</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-retaining_structure" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">retaining structure</span>, column, suspended <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-floor" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_3">floor</span>, other device or series of such devices may be constructed that enables the              <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-ground_floor" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_4" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_4">ground floor</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_5" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_5">building</span> to be raised more than 0,5 metres above <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-natural_ground_level" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_6" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_6">natural ground level</span>, provided that where the raising takes place, the            <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_7" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_7">height</span> must still be measured from <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-natural_ground_level" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_8" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_8">natural ground level</span>, excluding infill for a driveway; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">earth banks and/or retaining structures will be dependent on complying with engineering specifications and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">building</span> plan approval by the             <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">Municipality</span>.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_27" data-eId="sec_27"><h3>27. Boundary walls</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">In the absence of an approved <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-site_development_plan" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">site development plan</span>, architectural guidelines or relevant policy, following development parameters apply to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-boundary" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2">boundary</span> walls:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">Height</span><span class="akn-p">The maximum <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">height</span> in all cases is 2,1 metres.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Permeability</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">60% of a residential <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-street_boundary" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i__term_1">street boundary</span> wall must be permeable; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">80% of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-street_boundary" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1">street boundary</span> wall in other areas must be permeable.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_28" data-eId="sec_28"><h3>28. Maintenance of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_28__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__term_1">property</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_28__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_28__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Property must be properly maintained by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">owner</span> or occupier and may not</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">Contain an unsightly accumulation of papers, cartons, garden refuse, rubble or other waste material, as may be determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">Municipality</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">contain an accumulation of motor wrecks or un roadworthy vehicles or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-used" id="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">used</span> motor parts, unless these are part of a primary or consent use in          terms of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">zoning</span> scheme;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1" data-eId="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">contain outdoor storage of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_1">building</span> material, appliances or similar items unless these</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">form part of a primary or consent use in terms of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1">zoning</span> scheme;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">are temporarily being stored for the purpose of construction in accordance with a valid <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__term_1">building</span> plan approval; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">are being stored in conjunction with the holding of a yard or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-garage" id="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii__term_1">garage</span> sale with a duration of not more than two consecutive days.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_29" data-eId="sec_29"><h3>29. Parking of vehicles and water crafts in residential zones</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-motor_vehicle" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">motor vehicle</span> of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupant" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2">occupant</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dwelling_unit" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_3">dwelling unit</span> and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-used" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_4">used</span> for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-commercial" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_5">commercial</span> activities conducted away from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dwelling_unit" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_6">dwelling unit</span> may be parked on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_7">property</span> where the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-occupant" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_8" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_8">occupant</span> resides, provided that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">there is adequate space on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">property</span> concerned;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">no more than one <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-commercial" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">commercial</span> vehicle per <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dwelling_unit" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">dwelling unit</span> may be parked on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_3">property</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the gross weight of any such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-commercial" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">commercial</span> vehicle may not exceed 3 500 kg; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the parking space provided for a water craft may not exceed 8m ( 26ft) in width and 15m ( 59ft) in length.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_30" data-eId="sec_30"><h3>30. Mobile homes and caravans</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_30__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A recreation vehicle, including a mobile home, camp trailer or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-caravan" id="sec_30__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__term_1">caravan</span>, may not be <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-used" id="sec_30__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__term_2">used</span> for permanent habitation without the approval of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_30__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__term_3">Municipality</span>, unless the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_30__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__term_4">zoning</span> lawfully allows such activity.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_30__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following additional development parameters apply with regard to mobile homes approved to be placed on a land unit zoned for residential purposes:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the mobile home or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-caravan" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">caravan</span> must be sited on a foundation slab and properly anchored;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">solid perimeter skirting, of material and colour complementary to the mobile home or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-caravan" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">caravan</span>, must be provided from the bottom of the mobile         home to the ground surface; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">any structural additions must be of materials which, in the opinion of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">Municipality</span>, are compatible with the mobile home or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-caravan" id="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2">caravan</span>.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_31" data-eId="sec_31"><h3>31. Rooftop base telecommunication stations and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-satellite_dish_antenna" id="sec_31__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__term_1">satellite dish antenna</span> systems</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A rooftop base telecommunication station may not extend more than 3 metres in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_1">height</span> above the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_2">building</span> that it is attached to without the prior approval of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_3">Municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No rooftop base telecommunication station or transmission tower granted consent use in terms of this by-law may be modified or have its radio-frequency emissions altered without prior written approval from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following provisions apply with regard to decommissioned antennae or rooftop base telecommunication stations:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">owner</span> or operator must remove all decommissioned infrastructure;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if the site has been disturbed, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">owner</span> or operator must rehabilitate the site to its original state or to a state acceptable to the               <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2">Municipality</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1">owner</span> or operator fails to comply with paragraphs (a) or (b), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_2">Municipality</span> may remove that infrastructure, and rehabilitate the           site at the expense of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_3">owner</span> or operator.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-satellite_dish_antenna" id="sec_31__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_4__term_1">satellite dish antenna</span> with a diameter in excess of 1,5 metres must be placed in a position that minimises the visual impact on the surrounding area, to the satisfaction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_4__term_2">Municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Satellite dish antennas of 1,5 metres in diameter and smaller, and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-used" id="sec_31__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_5__term_1">used</span> solely for the purposes of television reception or telecommunication, do not require the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_5__term_2">Municipality</span>s approval and are excluded from <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_31__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_5__term_3">height</span> restrictions.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_32" data-eId="sec_32"><h3>32. Geysers and solar panels or similar infrastructure affixed to the roof of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_32__term_1" data-eId="sec_32__term_1">building</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_32__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_32__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any external geysers and associated equipment or solar panels or similar infrastructure affixed to the roof of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_32__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_32__hcontainer_1__term_1">building</span> may not at any point be more than 1,5 metres above the roof surface, measured perpendicularly from that surface.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_33" data-eId="sec_33"><h3>33. Equipment on top of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_33__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__term_1">building</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_33__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_33__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No elevator motor rooms, satellite dishes, ventilation shafts, water tanks, air conditioning plants or other equipment on top of a flat roofed <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_33__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__hcontainer_1__term_1">building</span> may exceed a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_33__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__hcontainer_1__term_2">height</span> of 2 metres above the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-wall_plate" id="sec_33__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_33__hcontainer_1__term_3">wall plate</span>.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_34" data-eId="sec_34"><h3>34. Parapet walls</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_34__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Parapet walls are restricted to 500 millimetres in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_34__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1__term_1">height</span> above the finished roof level immediately contiguous to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-parapet" id="sec_34__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1__term_2">parapet</span> except in the case where roof equipment as described under <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_34__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1__term_3">height</span> is hidden behind <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-parapet" id="sec_34__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1__term_4">parapet</span> walls, not exceeding 2 metres in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_34__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1__term_5">height</span>, which is to the satisfaction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_34__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1__term_6">Municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_34__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In the case of flats and non-residential buildings, the 2 metre <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-height" id="sec_34__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__term_1">height</span> limit under subsection (1) is considered to form part of the top <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-storey" id="sec_34__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__term_2">storey</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_35" data-eId="sec_35"><h3>35. Chimneys</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_35__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_35__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Chimneys may not extend higher than 1 metre above the highest point of the roof of a dwelling house or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dwelling_unit" id="sec_35__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__hcontainer_1__term_1">dwelling unit</span>.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_36" data-eId="sec_36"><h3>36. Telecommunication and electrical transmission lines</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_36__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_36__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any land unit, irrespective of its <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_36__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_36__hcontainer_1__term_1">zoning</span>, as a primary right, may allow telecommunication and electrical transmission lines to traverse it, as may be reasonably required by the municipality or a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_authority" id="sec_36__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_36__hcontainer_1__term_2">public authority</span>.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_37" data-eId="sec_37"><h3>37. Electronic or mechanical playing devices</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Electronic or mechanical playing devices are permitted in accordance with the applicable legislation and approved municipal policy.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_38" data-eId="sec_38"><h3>38. Utilisation of outbuildings</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_38__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_38__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-outbuilding" id="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_1">outbuilding</span> may be utilised for any purpose other than the purpose submitted in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_2">building</span> plans and approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_3">Municipality</span>, and an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-outbuilding" id="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_4">outbuilding</span> may not be utilised until the main buildings are completed or occupied, unless approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_5">Municipality</span>.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_39" data-eId="sec_39"><h3>39. Animals in urban areas</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_39__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_39__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No animals may be kept for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-commercial" id="sec_39__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_39__hcontainer_1__term_1">commercial</span> purposes on a land unit.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_40" data-eId="sec_40"><h3>40. Hobbies in single and general residential zones</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">When exercising a hobby in all single and general residential zones, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dominant_use" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">dominant use</span> of the dwelling house or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-dwelling_unit" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2">dwelling unit</span> must be for the living accommodation of a single <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-family" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_3">family</span>, provided that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">no portion of the dwelling, may be <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-used" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">used</span> for the purposes of a noxious trade, risk activity or sale of alcoholic beverages;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">in addition to paragraph (a), the following uses are not classified as hobbies:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">activities conforming to the definition of a shop;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">undertaker;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">animal care centres;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">escort agencies or adult entertainment;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">tow-in services;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_vi" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_vi"><span class="akn-num">(vi)</span><span class="akn-p">places of entertainment;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_vii" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_vii"><span class="akn-num">(vii)</span><span class="akn-p">hospitals or clinics;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_viii" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_viii"><span class="akn-num">(viii)</span><span class="akn-p">places of instruction;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ix" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ix"><span class="akn-num">(ix)</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-motor_vehicle" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ix__term_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ix__term_1">motor vehicle</span> repairs;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_x" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_x"><span class="akn-num">(x)</span><span class="akn-p">panel beating or spray painting;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xi" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xi"><span class="akn-num">(xi)</span><span class="akn-p">parcel delivery services;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xii" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xii"><span class="akn-num">(xii)</span><span class="akn-p">shooting ranges or shooting instructions;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xiii" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xiii"><span class="akn-num">(xiii)</span><span class="akn-p">butcheries;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xiv" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xiv"><span class="akn-num">(xiv)</span><span class="akn-p">taxi businesses;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xv" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xv"><span class="akn-num">(xv)</span><span class="akn-p">fishmongers;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xvi" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xvi"><span class="akn-num">(xvi)</span><span class="akn-p">vehicle rental agencies;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xvii" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xvii"><span class="akn-num">(xvii)</span><span class="akn-p">manufacturing of concrete products;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xviii" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xviii"><span class="akn-num">(xviii)</span><span class="akn-p">transport contractors;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xix" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xix"><span class="akn-num">(xix)</span><span class="akn-p">house shops;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xx" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xx"><span class="akn-num">(xx)</span><span class="akn-p">house taverns;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xxi" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xxi"><span class="akn-num">(xxi)</span><span class="akn-p">coal and wood merchants;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xxii" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xxii"><span class="akn-num">(xxii)</span><span class="akn-p">the training, breeding and/or coop facilities for homing pigeons; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xxiii" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xxiii"><span class="akn-num">(xxiii)</span><span class="akn-p">any other industry which, in the opinion of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xxiii__term_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xxiii__term_1">Municipality</span>, does not fit in the particular environment or is of such nature that it                 must be located on a suitably zoned <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises"
