id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xxiii__term_2" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_xxiii__term_2">premises</span>;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">no goods may publicly be displayed and no external evidence of the hobby may be visible from the street;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">no advertising may be displayed;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">any public exhibition of hobby items or activities on the residential <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_1">property</span> must:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">be preceded by a written consent from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i__term_1">Municipality</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">during such an event, temporary parking must be provided on the land unit in accordance with the parking requirements of this By-law and             appropriate traffic regulating measures must be put in place;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">an activity associated with a hobby may not occupy more than 25% of the total <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-floor" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_1">floor</span> area of the dwelling on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_2" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_2">property</span> or 60 m, including         storage;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__term_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g__term_1">Municipality</span> may restrict the operating hours relating to the hobby, if the activity proves to be a nuisance to residents in the area;           and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">any new <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-structure" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_h__term_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_h__term_1">structure</span>, or alteration to the existing dwelling or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-outbuilding" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_h__term_2" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_h__term_2">outbuilding</span>, must conform to the residential character of the area concerned.</span></span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_8" data-eId="chp_8"><h2>Chapter 8<br>Parking and loading</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_41" data-eId="sec_41"><h3>41. Off-street parking requirements</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_41__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_41__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If parking requirements are not stipulated for a particular use, or in terms of a specific condition imposed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span>, parking must be provided at a minimum ratio in accordance with the table entitled Minimum off-street parking requirements</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">Municipality</span> must determine off-street parking requirements for land uses not stipulated in the table Minimum off-street parking                requirements;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the second column in the table Minimum off-street parking requirements refers to requirements that apply to areas with standard parking            needs, or if public transport is not specifically promoted or available; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1" data-eId="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">off-street parking space must be provided</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__term_1">property</span> for which parking is required;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">subject to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii__term_1">Municipality</span>s approval, in public parking facilities available in the vicinity; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_41__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">in accordance with the table Minimum off-street parking requirements.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><h3 class="akn-crossHeading" id="sec_41__hcontainer_2" data-eId="sec_41__hcontainer_2">Minimum off-street parking requirements</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_41__hcontainer_3" data-eId="sec_41__hcontainer_3" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><table id="sec_41__hcontainer_3__table_1" data-eId="sec_41__hcontainer_3__table_1">

<td><span class="akn-p">1 bay per 200m <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-GLA" id="sec_41__hcontainer_3__table_1__term_26" data-eId="sec_41__hcontainer_3__table_1__term_26">GLA</span></span></td>
</tr>
</table></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_42" data-eId="sec_42"><h3>42. Alternative parking supply</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_42__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">As an alternative to compliance with the off-street parking requirements in terms of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">zoning</span> scheme, an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">owner</span> may, with the approval of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">Municipality</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">acquire an area of land sufficient for the permanent parking requirements elsewhere, in a location approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">Municipality</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">acquire permanent rights to a parking facility or portion of a parking facility elsewhere, in a location approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">Municipality</span>, and           must register a notarial tie or servitude against that land or parking facility to link the properties concerned for the purpose of parking,         and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">owner</span> must cause the parking concerned to be constructed and maintained in accordance with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_3">Municipality</span>s requirements and               approval.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_42__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The cost of registration of the notarial tie or servitude referred to in paragraph (1)(b) must be borne by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_42__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_42__subsec_2__term_1">owner</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_43" data-eId="sec_43"><h3>43. Combined parking requirements</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_43__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_43__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_43__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_43__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If two or more uses combine to share a common parking area, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_43__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_43__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may approve parking requirements that provide less than the quantum of the parking required for individual uses provided that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_43__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_43__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_43__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_43__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">Municipality</span> is satisfied that the utilisation of the same parking area by the different use types or activities in the zones will not           result in a concurrent use of the parking area; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_43__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_43__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">bays intended for combined uses may not subsequently be reallocated to other uses without the approval of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_43__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_43__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">Municipality</span>.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_44" data-eId="sec_44"><h3>44. Site access and exits</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_44__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_44__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may require compliance with standard municipal or provincial access spacing guidelines.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_44__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No access may be closer than 10 metres from an intersection as defined by the prolongation of street boundaries, except for industrial-zoned properties, where the distance may be 15 metres.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_44__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_44__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> may restrict or prohibit access if a pedestrian or traffic hazard is created or is likely to be created.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_44__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Vehicle entrances and exit ways to and from a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__term_1">property</span> must conform to the following requirements:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-motor_vehicle" id="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1">motor vehicle</span> carriageway crossings must be limited to one per site per <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_street" id="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_2">public street</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-road" id="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_3">road</span> abutting the site;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">notwithstanding paragraph (a) above, where the total length of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-street_boundary" id="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1">street boundary</span> of a site exceeds 30 metres, in length, one additional            <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-carriageway_crossing" id="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_2">carriageway crossing</span> may be permitted, provided that no two carriageway crossings are closer than 12 metres to each other;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the minimum and maximum widths of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-motor_vehicle" id="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_1">motor vehicle</span> carriageway crossings must be in accordance with the table titled Width of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-motor_vehicle" id="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_2">motor vehicle</span>            carriageway crossings; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_44__subsec_4__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the minimum width of a panhandle access may not be less than 4 metres wide.</span></span></span></span></section><h3 class="akn-crossHeading" id="sec_44__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_44__hcontainer_1">Width of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-motor_vehicle" id="sec_44__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__hcontainer_1__term_1">motor vehicle</span> carriageway crossings</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_44__hcontainer_2" data-eId="sec_44__hcontainer_2" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><table id="sec_44__hcontainer_2__table_1" data-eId="sec_44__hcontainer_2__table_1">
<tr>
<th><span class="akn-p">Type of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-carriageway_crossing" id="sec_44__hcontainer_2__table_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_44__hcontainer_2__table_1__term_1">carriageway crossing</span></span></th>
<th><span class="akn-p">Minimum width</span></th>
<th><span class="akn-p">Maximum width</span></th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">Single entrance or exit way</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">2,7 metres</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">6 metres</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">Combined entrance and exit way</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">5 metres</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">10 metres</span></td>
</tr>
</table></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_45" data-eId="sec_45"><h3>45. Parking layout requirements</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following parking layout requirements apply unless otherwise stated in this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">zoning</span> scheme:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">parking layout configurations, minimum dimensions and ramps to a parking area must be in accordance with this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">zoning</span> scheme or an approved           <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-site_development_plan" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">site development plan</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the layout of any parking area, except for parking in Single Residential Zone I, Single Residential Zone II and General Residential Zone I,          must ensure that vehicles can readily leave the site without reversing across the sidewalk, unless otherwise approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">Municipality</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a tandem bay accommodating two motor vehicles is regarded as one bay for the purposes of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-zoning" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">zoning</span> scheme, except for single residential           zones, where a tandem bay is regarded as two bays;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">visitor parking bays must be clearly demarcated, readily visible and accessible to visitors, and preferably grouped together;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">parking areas must be <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-used" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1">used</span> for the parking of vehicles which are lawfully allowed on them, and any activity which causes an obstruction for          vehicular traffic or pedestrian use of the sidewalk is prohibited;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">parking areas must be constructed and maintained in a state suitable for the parking and movement of vehicles;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">control of access to and reservation of parking bays and / or areas is not permitted unless written approval has been obtained from the              <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_1">Municipality</span>; either through an approved <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-site_development_plan" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_2">site development plan</span> or other written approval; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">despite paragraphs (a) to (g), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_h__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_h__term_1">Municipality</span> may lay down more restrictive requirements related to parking, site access or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-motor_vehicle" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_h__term_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_h__term_2">motor vehicle</span>          <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-carriageway_crossing" id="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_h__term_3" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_1__list_1__item_h__term_3">carriageway crossing</span>, if it considers this to be necessary from a pedestrian or traffic safety point of view.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may require an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">applicant</span> to submit a parking layout plan indicating</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the way in which it is proposed that motor vehicles park;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the means of entrance and exit from parking areas;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-landscaping" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">landscaping</span> proposals;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">construction details; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">any other information that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1">Municipality</span> deems necessary relevant to the provision of parking.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_45__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_45__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_45__subsec_3__term_1">Municipality</span> may approve or refuse the parking layout plan and impose conditions of approval.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_46" data-eId="sec_46"><h3>46. Parking for the physically disabled</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_46__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_46__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may require parking suitable for use by persons with physical disabilities to be provided on any land unit in order to ensure easy and convenient access for such persons to services and facilities generally open to the public and to residential uses.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_46__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In any parking facility serving the public, parking for persons with physical disabilities must be provided in accordance with the table entitled Physically disabled accessible parking.</span></span></section><h3 class="akn-crossHeading" id="sec_46__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_46__hcontainer_1">Physically disabled accessible parking</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_46__hcontainer_2" data-eId="sec_46__hcontainer_2" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><table id="sec_46__hcontainer_2__table_1" data-eId="sec_46__hcontainer_2__table_1">
<tr>
<th><span class="akn-p">Total no of parking bays</span></th>
<th><span class="akn-p">Required number of bays accessible to the physically disabled</span></th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">1-50</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">1</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">51-100</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">2</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">101-150</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">3</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">151-200</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">4</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">For every additional 100 bays</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">1 additional <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-parking_bay" id="sec_46__hcontainer_2__table_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__hcontainer_2__table_1__term_1">parking bay</span></span></td>
</tr>
</table></span></span><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_46__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Parking for the physically disabled must comply with the following requirements:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">parking bays must be a minimum of 3,7 metres in width and 5 metres in length;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">parking and access aisles must be level;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">parking bays must be located as near as possible to accessible <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-building" id="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1">building</span> or site entrances and must be located to provide convenient access to         kerb ramps;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-parking_bay" id="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_1">parking bay</span> reserved for physically disabled persons must be marked on the parking surface with the international symbol for disabled           accessibility;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">additional signage indicating the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-parking_bay" id="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_1">parking bay</span> as reserved for exclusive use by persons with physical disabilities may be required by the             <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_2" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_2">Municipality</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">if five or fewer parking bays are provided, at least one bay must be 4 metres wide and marked to provide a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-parking_bay" id="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_3__list_1__item_f__term_1">parking bay</span> of 2,5 metres with an         access aisle of 1,5 metres, but the bay need not be reserved exclusively for persons with physical disabilities.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_46__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_46__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Parking for persons with physical disabilities must count towards fulfilling off-street parking requirements.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_47" data-eId="sec_47"><h3>47. Motorcycle and bicycle parking spaces</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_47__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_47__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may require that parking be provided for motorcycles and bicycles.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_47__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">For every 4 motorcycle and 6 bicycle parking spaces provided, a credit of 1 <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-parking_bay" id="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">parking bay</span> may be given towards applicable parking requirements, provided that</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the total credit may not exceed 2,5% of the parking bays required;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the minimum dimension for a motorcycle space is 2,2 metres in length and 1 metre in width; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the minimum dimension for a bicycle space is 2 metres in length and 0,6 metres in width.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_47__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_47__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Signage, bollards and racks or other devices for storing bicycles and enabling motorcyclists to make use of such bays must be installed.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_48" data-eId="sec_48"><h3>48. Loading requirements</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_48__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Unless the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_48__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_1__term_1">Municipality</span> grants approval to waive this requirement, loading bays must be provided in accordance with the table entitled Minimum off-street <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-loading_bay" id="sec_48__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_1__term_2">loading bay</span> requirements.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_48__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_48__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_2__term_1">Municipality</span> may determine off-street loading requirements for uses not stipulated in the table.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_48__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_48__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following minimum requirements apply to loading bays:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_48__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-loading_bay" id="sec_48__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">loading bay</span> must measure not less than 4,5 metres  10 metres for perpendicular loading, and 2,5 metres  12 metres for parallel loading;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_48__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">no <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-carriageway_crossing" id="sec_48__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">carriageway crossing</span> to be accessed by loading vehicles may be less than 3 metres in width, and no combined entrance and exit way may be          less than 6 metres in width; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_48__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_48__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">covered loading areas must have a minimum headroom of 3,7 metres.</span></span></span></span></section><h3 class="akn-crossHeading" id="sec_48__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_48__hcontainer_1">Minimum off-street <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-loading_bay" id="sec_48__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__hcontainer_1__term_1">loading bay</span> requirements</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_48__hcontainer_2" data-eId="sec_48__hcontainer_2" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><table id="sec_48__hcontainer_2__table_1" data-eId="sec_48__hcontainer_2__table_1">
<tr>

<th style="width: 30.3621%;"><span class="akn-p">Floor area (m)</span></th>
<th style="width: 36.0724%;"><span class="akn-p">Number of loading bays</span></th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">Offices</span></td>
<td style="width:30.3621%"><span class="akn-p">05 000<br>5 00115 000<br>15 00130 000<br>Every additional 30 000 or part thereof</span></td>
<td style="width:36.0724%"><span class="akn-p">0<br>1<br>2<br>1 additional bay</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">Business <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_48__hcontainer_2__table_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_48__hcontainer_2__table_1__term_1">premises</span> other than offices, supermarket, industry</span></td>
<td style="width:30.3621%"><span class="akn-p">01 000<br>1 0012 500<br>2 5015 000<br>5 00110 000<br>Every additional 10 000 or part thereof</span></td>
<td style="width:36.0724%"><span class="akn-p">0<br>1<br>2<br>3<br>1 additional bay</span></td>
</tr>

</tr>
</table></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_9" data-eId="chp_9"><h2>Chapter 9<br>Refuse rooms and service yards</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_49" data-eId="sec_49"><h3>49. Refuse rooms</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_49__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_49__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may, for the purposes of collecting refuse, require the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2">owner</span> to install a refuse receptacle on a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_3">property</span> which</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">is of sufficient size to accommodate the refuse generated from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">property</span> for one week;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">is located adjacent to a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_street" id="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">public street</span>, or in a position which will provide acceptable access to a refuse collection vehicle;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">is designed in a manner that is architecturally compatible with the other structures on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">property</span> and will screen refuse bins from public         view; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">comply with any other conditions or standard requirements that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_49__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">Municipality</span> may impose relating to access, health, pollution control,            safety or aesthetics.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_50" data-eId="sec_50"><h3>50. Service yards</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_50__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_50__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_50__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_50__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_50__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">Municipality</span> may require the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_50__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_50__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2">owner</span> to install a screened area providing utility services like washing lines for residential developments, which</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_50__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_50__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">is designed in a manner that is architecturally compatible with the other structures on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_50__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">property</span> and will screen refuse bins from public         view; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_50__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_50__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">complies with any other conditions or standard requirements that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Municipality" id="sec_50__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_50__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">Municipality</span> may impose relating to access, health, pollution control,          safety or aesthetics.</span></span></span></span></span></section></section></span><span class="akn-attachments"><div class="akn-attachment" id="att_1" data-eId="att_1">
<h2 class="akn-heading">Schedule 1</h2>
<h2 class="akn-subheading">Use zones table</h2>
<span class="akn-doc" data-name="schedule"><span class="akn-mainBody"><span class="akn-hcontainer" id="att_1/hcontainer_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><table id="att_1/hcontainer_1__table_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__table_1">
<tr>
<th class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">1</span></th>
<th class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">2</span></th>
<th class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">3</span></th>
</tr>
<tr>
<th class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">Zoning</span></th>
<th class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">Primary use</span></th>
<th class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">Consent use</span></th>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3" class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">AGRICULTURAL ZONES</span></th></tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Agricultural Zone I (AZ1)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to promote and protect agriculture on farms as an important economic, environmental and cultural resource. Limited provision is made for non-agricultural uses to provide rural communities in more remote areas with the opportunity to increase the economic potential of their properties, provided these uses do not present a significant negative impact on the primary agricultural resource.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary use</b><br> Agriculture<br> Farm shop<br> Function venue<br> Guest house<br> Bed Breakfast<br> Plant nursery</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Additional dwelling units<br> Airfield<br> Animal care centre<br> Aqua-culture<br> Farm Shop<br> Freestanding base telecommunication station<br> Off road trail<br> Quarry<br> Renewable energy structure<br> Tourist facilities<br> Utility service<br> Crche<br> Farmers Market</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Agricultural Zone II (AZII)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to accommodate larger residential properties, which may be used for limited agriculture, but primarily serve as places of residence for people who seek a rural lifestyle. Such properties are often found close to towns and villages, and new smallholding areas should only be permitted within an acknowledged, demarcated urban area.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary use</b><br> Smallholding<br> Farm shop<br> Guest house<br> Bed Breakfast<br> Plant nursery<br> Riding school<br> Second dwelling unit</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Agriculture industry<br> Animal care centre<br> Aqua-culture<br> Freestanding base telecommunication station<br> Intensive animal farming<br> Intensive horticulture Quarry<br> Renewable energy structure<br> Rooftop base telecommunication station<br> Tourist facilities<br> Utility service<br> Crche<br> Farmers market</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Agriculture Zone III (AZIII)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The purpose of this zone is to support the governments rural land development programme and provide for the establishment of worker accommodation outside conventional towns. This will help to address the accommodation needs of workers and their dependants in rural areas such as farms, forestry and conservation areas.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary use</b><br> Agri-village</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Freestanding base telecommunication station<br> Rooftop base telecommunication station</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3" class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">SINGLE RESIDENTIAL ZONES</span></th></tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Single Residential Zone I (SRZI)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide for residential development where the predominant type of accommodation is a dwelling house for a single family, where each dwelling has its own land unit, and adequate outdoor space. Limited employment and additional accommodation opportunities are possible as primary or consent uses, provided that the dominant use of the property remains residential, and impacts of such uses do not adversely affect the quality and character of the surrounding residential environment.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary use</b><br> Dwelling house</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Crche<br> Guest house<br> Halfway house<br> Second dwelling unit</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Single Residential Zone II (SRZII)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide for upgrading and incremental housing from informal settlements to formal settlements and also to allow formal as well as informal housing types on a single erf. In recognition of the realities of poor and marginalised communities, development management provisions are not restrictive and local employment generation is encouraged within this zone.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary use</b><br> Shelter<br> Dwelling house</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> House Shop</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3" class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">GENERAL RESIDENTIAL ZONES</span></th></tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">General Residential Zone I (GRZI)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to facilitate low intensity densification in designated areas, which will not have an adverse effect on the character of the existing built area and may contribute to the optimal utilisation of land and infrastructure. The residential development consists of two dwelling units in a single structure, each of which may accommodate a single family. Individual ownership of the units will be allowed through a sectional title scheme. Architecturally, the dwelling units will be uniform and will be developed to the same scale and extent.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary use</b><br> Double dwelling house</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Home occupation</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">General Residential Zone II (GRZII)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to encourage residential development of a medium density, with a coordinated design, and to accommodate group housing where special attention is given to aesthetics, architectural form and the inter-relationship between components of the group housing scheme. Group housing may be located in single residential areas in places where an increased density is desirable, including along main roads, near local shopping centres and other activity nodes, and also preferably near to public open spaces.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary use</b><br> Group housing</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Flats<br> Home occupation<br> Retirement resort</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">General Residential Zone III (GRZIII)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to encourage residential development of a greater density than for General Residential Zone II, while retaining the emphasis on design coordination and a modest scale in terms of height. This zone has particular location requirements, such as proximity to transport and amenities, and should not be randomly located without due consideration of the availability of open space and community facilities. Town housing may be located in and around central business areas, near high density nodes and along activity axis such as railway lines and main traffic routes, where flats are often found.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary use</b><br> Town housing</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Flats<br> Home occupation<br> Retirement resort</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">General Residential Zone IV (GRZIV)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to promote higher density residential development. The dominant use within this zone must be residential, but limited mixed-use development is possible with the Municipalitys consent. This zone has particular location requirements, such as proximity to transport and amenities, and should not be randomly located without due consideration of the availability of open space and community facilities.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary use</b><br> Flats</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Backpackers lodge<br> Boarding house<br> Convenience shop<br> Home occupation<br> Renewable energy structure<br> Retirement resort<br> Rooftop base telecommunication station</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">General Residential Zone V (GRZV)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide a temporary residence for transient guests in an appropriately scaled establishment where lodging and meals are provided and which may include a small conference/training facility that also caters for business meetings.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary use</b><br> Guest lodge<br> Backpackers lodge</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Restaurant</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">General Residential Zone VI (GRZVI)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide a temporary residence for transient guests, where lodging and meals are provided, and may include a restaurant and conference facilities. Outside towns it should only be considered in identified tourism areas or within resorts.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary use</b><br> Hotel</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Backpackers lodge<br> Renewable energy structure<br> Rooftop base telecommunication station<br> Shop</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3" class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">BUSINESS ZONES</span></th></tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Business Zone I (BZI)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide for intensive business and mixed-use development with relatively few restrictions in order to promote urban vitality and economic growth.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary use</b><br> Business premises</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Adult entertainment<br>Adult services<br> Adult shop<br> Freestanding base telecommunication station<br> Helicopter landing pad<br> Motor repair garage<br> Open air motor vehicle display<br> Place of entertainment<br> Renewable energy structure<br> Transport use<br> Warehouse<br> Service trade</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Business Zone II (BZII)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide for the retail sale of goods and services to the public.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary use</b><br> Shop</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Conference facility<br> Flats<br> Freestanding base telecommunication station<br> Liquor store<br> Open air motor vehicle display<br> Place of assembly<br> Place of entertainment<br> Place of instruction<br> Renewable energy structure<br> Restaurant<br> Rooftop base telecommunication station<br> Service station<br> Supermarket<br> Office<br> Plant nursery</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Business Zone III (BZIII)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide for low intensity commercial and mixed-use development, which serves local neighbourhood needs for convenience goods and personal services. Such development should be limited in scale and nature and capable of integration into the adjacent residential neighbourhood, without adversely affecting the amenity of the residential neighbourhood. While mixed use development is encouraged, care must be taken not to compromise business operations.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary use</b><br> Neighbourhood shop</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Flats<br> Liquor store<br> Restaurant<br> Service trade<br> Supermarket</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Business Zone IV (BZIV)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide an intermediate zone, which can, if required, act as a buffer or interface between high- and medium-intensity business zones, and residential zones. Retail activities are limited to those which are ancillary to the dominant permitted uses, namely offices and flats. In order to protect the amenity of adjacent residential areas, appropriate levels of landscaping and environmental management are required.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary use</b><br> Offices</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Flats<br> Institution<br> Place of assembly<br> Place of entertainment<br> Place of instruction<br> Renewable energy structure<br> Restaurant<br> Rooftop base telecommunication station<br> Shop<br> Supermarket</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Business Zone V (BZV)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide for large-scale regional retail facilities that exceed the floor area of shops and supermarkets aimed at the local market in general. These facilities may offer a diverse range of products under one roof and supply products to individuals as well as wholesale trade. Such facilities may be developed as a power centre. Specific consideration should be given to the locality and placement of these facilities with consideration of their regional significance and accessibility as well as possible impact on existing nodal areas.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses</b><br> Big box retail<br> Shop</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Place of entertainment<br> Renewable energy<br> Structure<br> Rooftop base telecommunication station<br> Warehouse</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Business Zone VI (BZVI)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide opportunities in urban areas for service stations, motor repair garages and associated facilities which have specific vehicle access requirements and potential negative impacts on adjoining areas.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses</b><br> Service station</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Motor repair garage<br> Shop<br> Truck stop</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3" class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">INDUSTRIAL ZONES</span></th></tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Industrial Zone 1 (IZI)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to accommodate industry uses and service trades that may be carried out without nuisance to other properties or the general public. Such uses may be located next to business uses and in close proximity to residential areas, and do not present a potential negative impact on the character or amenity of such areas.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary use</b><br> Light industry</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Adult entertainment<br> Adult services<br> Adult shop<br> Aqua-culture<br> Caretakers quarters<br> Convenience shop<br> Liquor store<br> Office<br> Place of entertainment<br> Renewable energy structure<br> Truck stop<br> Funeral parlour</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Industrial Zone II (IZII)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to accommodate all forms of industry, except noxious trade and risk activity, in order to promote the manufacturing sector of the economy. Some allowance is made for non-industrial activities, but these should not compromise the general use of the area zoned for industry. It is accepted that the intensive nature of the industrial activity or the scale of the operation could generate some negative impact on adjacent properties.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary use</b><br> Industry</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Abattoir<br> Adult entertainment<br> Adult services<br> Aqua-culture<br> Container site<br> Convenience shop<br> Crematorium<br> Helicopter landing pad<br> Liquor store<br> Office<br> Place of entertainment<br> Renewable energy structure<br> Restaurant<br> Scrap yard<br> Truck stop</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Industrial Zone III(IZIII)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide for those industries which are noxious in terms of smell, product, waste or other objectionable consequence of their operation, or which carry a high risk in the event of fire or accident. While other uses are permitted with consent, the Municipality must ensure there is sufficient capacity for noxious trade in the limited areas suitable for this zone. A noxious trade should not be located close to residential areas.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses</b><br> Noxious trade</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"> Consent uses<br> Container site<br> Convenience shop<br> Helicopter landing pad<br> Industry<br> Liquor store<br> Motor repair garage<br> Renewable energy structure<br> Scrap yard<br> Service station<br> Transport use</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Industrial Zone IV (IZIV)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide for the use of land for the extraction of minerals and raw materials and, to a limited extent, associated business operations. This zone is intended for operations of a more permanent nature as opposed to temporary, short-term mining or prospecting activities.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses</b><br> Mine<br> Industry</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b></span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3" class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">COMMUNITY ZONES</span></th></tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Community Zone I (CZI)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide for educational facilities of all kinds, but controlled provision is made for other compatible community uses.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses</b><br> Place of instruction</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Conference facility<br> Freestanding base telecommunication station<br> Institution<br> Place of assembly<br> Rooftop base telecommunication station</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Community Zone II (CZII)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide for places where communities can congregate and worship according to the custom of their specific faith or religion.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses</b><br> Place of worship<br> Garden of remembrance<br> Wall of remembrance<br> Crche</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Cemetery<br> Institution<br> Place of instruction<br> Rooftop base telecommunication station</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Community Zone III (CZIII)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide for a wide range of institutional uses including facilities for health, education and worship.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses</b><br> Institution</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses </b><br> Correctional facility<br> Rooftop base telecommunication station</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3" class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">RESORT ZONE</span></th></tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Resort Zone I (RZI)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to promote tourist and holiday facilities in areas with special environmental or recreational attributes, and to encourage general public access to these facilities. At the same time, care should be exercised to minimise potential negative impacts of development on fragile environments. The guiding principle should be that a resort must not detract from the amenity that attracted the holiday facilities in the first place, nor should it cause a public nuisance for other people living and working in the vicinity. This zone should only be used in exceptional cases and is normally applicable to tourist developments outside established, built-up areas.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses </b><br> Tourist accommodation</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Consent uses<br> Hotel<br> Tourist facilities<br> Wellness centre<br> Function venue</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Resort Zone II (RZII)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to reserve a zoning for existing resorts situated outside the urban edge, approved in terms of Section 8 of the Land Use Planning Ordinance, 1985 under the Resort II zoning. Furthermore, to provide for new resort development which will be required to consist of at least a 50% Resort Zone I component or more. This is to ensure that a public resort function is incorporated in developments within this zoning category.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses </b><br> Holiday housing</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses </b><br> Hotel<br> Tourist facilities<br> Wellness centre</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3" class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">OPEN SPACE ZONES</span></th></tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">OPEN SPACE ZONE I (OSZI)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide for active and passive recreational areas on public land, in order to promote recreation, and enhance the aesthetic appearance of an area.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses </b><br> Public open space</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> Air and underground rights<br> Cemetery x Environmental facilities<br> Informal trading<br> Tourist facilities<br> Urban agriculture<br> Utility service</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">OPEN SPACE ZONE II (OSZII)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide for active and passive recreational areas on private land, in order to promote recreation and enhance the aesthetic appearance of an area.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses </b><br> Private open space</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses </b><br> Cemetery<br> Environmental facilities<br> Informal trading<br> Plant nursery<br> Tourist facilities<br> Urban agriculture<br> Utility service</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">OPEN SPACE ZONE III (OSZIII)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide for the conservation of natural resources in areas that have not been proclaimed as nature areas (non-statutory conservation), in order to sustain flora and fauna and protect areas of undeveloped landscape including woodlands, ridges, wetlands and the coastline. A range of consent uses is provided to supplement and support the main objective of this zone.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses </b><br> Nature conservation area</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses </b><br> Environmental facilities<br> Harvesting of natural resources<br> Tourist facilities<br> Utility service</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">OPEN SPACE ZONE IV (OSZIV)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">The objective of this zone is to provide for the conservation of natural resources in areas that have been proclaimed as nature areas (statutory conservation), in order to sustain flora and fauna and protect areas of undeveloped landscape including woodlands, ridges, wetlands and the coastline. A range of consent uses is provided to supplement and support the main objective of this zone.</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses </b><br> Nature reserve</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses </b><br> Tourist accommodation<br> Tourist facilities<br> Utility service<br> Conference Facility<br> Function Venue</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3" class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">TRANSPORT AND UTILITY ZONES</span></th></tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">TRANSPORT ZONE I (TUZI)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to reserve land for transportation systems, excluding public streets, but including all other transport undertakings.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses</b><br> Transport use</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses </b><br> Air and underground rights<br> Airfield<br> Airport<br> Business premises<br> Conference facility<br> Container site<br> Helicopter landing pad<br> Hotel<br> Industry<br> Informal trading<br> Motor repair garage<br> Service station<br> Warehouse</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">TRANSPORT ZONE II (TUZII)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide for public streets, whether constructed or still to be constructed, as well as infrastructure associated with such streets. Provision is also made for the temporary use of the land unit for other purposes as may be approved by the Municipality.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses </b><br> Public street</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses </b><br> Air and underground rights<br> Informal trading<br> Multiple parking garage</span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">TRANSPORT ZONE III (TUZIII)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to provide private roads for the passage or parking of motor vehicles, which is privately owned and does not vest in the Municipality or any other public authority.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses </b><br> Private road</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b></span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">AUTHORITY ZONE (AUZI)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to reserve land for uses normally undertaken by central, provincial and municipal government agencies as well as land for utility services such as electrical substations, and which do not fall into another zoning category. Some flexibility for the use of land and development parameters is provided.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses </b><br> Authority use<br> Utility service</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses </b></span></td>
</tr>
<tr><th colspan="3" class="akn--text-center"><span class="akn-p">UNDETERMINED ZONE</span></th></tr>
<tr><th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">UNDETERMINED USE ZONE (USZI)</span></th></tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"><i>The objective of this zone is to enable the Municipality to defer a decision regarding a specific land use and development management provisions until the circumstances affecting the land unit have been properly investigated; or until the owner of the land makes an application for rezoning; or a zoning determination is made by the Municipality. The objective of this zone is furthermore to create a zone to which land could revert back to when rights under current zonings, other than Single Residential Zone I, were not exercised, especially in cases where changes in the planning context occurred since the current zoning was granted.</i></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Primary uses </b><br> None</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p"><b>Consent uses</b><br> None</span></td>
</tr>
</table>
