<div class="akn-attachment" id="att_2" data-eId="att_2">
<h2 class="akn-heading">Schedule 2</h2>
<h2 class="akn-subheading">Land use descriptions and development parameters</h2>
<span class="akn-doc" data-name="schedule"><span class="akn-mainBody"><span class="akn-hcontainer" id="att_2/hcontainer_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p"><b>abattoir</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description: </b> abattoir is a place where animals are slaughtered and prepared for distribution to butchery shops and food markets.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to industry apply, and in the case where it is located on a farm, those applicable to agricultural industry apply for an abattoir.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>additional dwelling unit</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> additional dwelling unit is a dwelling unit that may be erected on an agricultural land unit with the consent of the Municipality, in addition to a primary dwelling house or agricultural worker accommodation for bona fide agricultural workers, or both, provided that</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">one additional unit can be allowed in all cases as a consent use, irrespective of the size of the agricultural land unit;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">further additional dwelling units can be allowed at a ratio of one additional dwelling unit per 10 ha, calculated on the basis of all additional dwelling units on the agricultural land unit, up to a maximum of five (5) additional dwelling units per agricultural land unit;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">an additional unit may not be erected within 1 km of the high water mark of the sea or a tidal river except where a proclaimed township is situated between the additional dwelling unit and the sea or tidal river;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">one additional dwelling unit may be erected within the 1km high water mark of the sea or a tidal river, provided that the additional dwelling unit is attached to the main house and does not exceed a floor area of 60m; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">additional dwelling units may not be alienated separately.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_2" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_2"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The development parameters applicable to agriculture apply, together with the following additional development parameters for additional dwelling units. Additional dwelling units may be erected with the consent of Municipality provided that</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_2__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_2__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a dwelling for a person engaged in bona fide agricultural activities on the land unit and which is permanently occupied by that person is not regarded as an additional dwelling unit;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_2__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_2__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the total floor space of an additional dwelling may not exceed 175 m, which includes the floor space in all ancillary buildings;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_2__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_2__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">an additional dwelling must be constructed in a style that is similar to the architecture of the main dwelling house, unless otherwise permitted by the Municipality;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_2__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_2__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">The height of a dwelling house and additional dwelling may not exceed 6 metres from the base to the wall plate in all cases and 8,5 metres to the ridge of the roof in the case of a pitched roof;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_2__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_2__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">an additional dwelling that is contained within the same building as a dwelling house must be designed so that the building appears to be a single dwelling house; provided that both units may have a ground floor, or one unit may be on the ground floor and the other unit above;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_2__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_2__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">the existence of an additional dwelling may not in itself be sufficient reason for the Municipality to grant an application in terms of the Planning By-law to subdivide the land unit containing the dwelling units; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>adult entertainment</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_3" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_3"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> adult entertainment</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_3__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_3__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">means the use of property for adult film theatres or strip clubs where sexually explicit, live or recorded shows are displayed; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_3__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_3__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include adult services or an adult shop.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to business premises apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>adult services</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_4" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_4"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> adult services</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_4__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_4__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">means the use of property for massage parlours or escort agencies, unless the services form part of a medical or therapeutic service provided by a registered medical practitioner or similar registered professional person; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_4__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_4__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include adult entertainment or an adult shop.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to business premises apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>adult shop</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_5" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_5"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> adult shop</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_5__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_5__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">means the use of property for the retail sale of pornographic, sexually explicit or erotic material, whether or not such material is displayed for sale, unless such material forms part of a medical or therapeutic service provided by a registered medical practitioner or similar registered professional person; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_5__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_5__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include adult entertainment or adult services.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to business premises apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>agricultural industry</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_6" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_6"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> agricultural industry</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_6__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_6__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">means an enterprise for the processing of agricultural products from a localised area in close proximity to the land unit if the agricultural products are grown or produced, and if processing in that proximity is necessary due to the nature, perishability and fragility of the agricultural products;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_6__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_6__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">includes a winery, dairy, distillery, packing store, the bottling of spring water, an abattoir and a saw mill; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_6__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_6__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include a service trade.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_7" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_7"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The development parameters applicable to agriculture apply. The municipality may approve a consent use application for an agricultural industry on land in an agricultural zone, provided that</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_7__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_7__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the agricultural industry does not adversely affect the agricultural potential of the property; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_7__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_7__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the area allocated for purposes of an agricultural industry is clearly identified on a land survey diagram or site development plan.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>agricultural worker accommodation</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> agricultural worker accommodation means accommodation provided for bona fide agricultural workers, including accommodation for labourers and farm managers, as determined by the Municipality based on the extent of the bona fide agricultural activities on the land unit.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_8" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_8"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The development parameters applicable to agriculture apply with the following additional development parameters:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_8__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_8__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the number of units must be reasonably connected to the bona fide agricultural activities on the land unit as determined in consultation with the Department of Agriculture; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_8__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_8__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">no agricultural worker accommodation may be erected within 1 km of the high water mark of the sea or water course (as defined by the National Environmental Management Act, 1998 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1998/107" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1998/107">Act 107 of 1998</a>)).</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>agriculture</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_9" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_9"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> agriculture means the cultivation of land for raising crops and other plants, including plantations, the keeping and breeding of animals, birds or bees, stud farming, game farming, intensive horticulture; intensive animal farming; a riding school or natural veld, and</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">includes</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the harvesting, packing, cooling, storing, sorting, and packaging of agricultural produce grown on that land unit and surrounding or nearby farms;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">harvesting of natural resources, which are limited to living organisms, for delivery to the market;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">agricultural buildings or infrastructure that are reasonably connected with the main farming activities, including a dwelling house, agricultural worker accommodation, packing stores and rooftop base telecommunication stations;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">telecommunication and electricity transmission lines; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a__list_1__item_v" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">agricultural industry;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_9__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_9__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include aquaculture; an abattoir, a farm shop, an animal care centre, any mining activity, and renewable energy structures for commercial purposes.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_10" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_10"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following development parameters apply:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_10__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_10__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">Building lines</span><span class="akn-p">The road or street and common boundary building lines are 30 metres.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_10__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_10__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_10__item_b__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_10__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Height</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_10__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_10__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The height of a dwelling house and additional dwelling may not exceed 6 metres from the base to the wall plate in all cases and 8,5 metres to the ridge of the roof in the case of a pitched roof.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_10__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_10__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">Agricultural buildings other than dwelling houses may not exceed a height of 15 metres to the top of the roof.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_10__item_b__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_10__item_b__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">Earth banks and retaining structures which in the opinion of Municipality are associated with bona fide agricultural activities are exempt from the general provisions in this regard in this by-law.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_10__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_10__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">Site development plan</span><span class="akn-p">For any development in this zone, including any part of the land not zoned Agriculture, a site development plan must be submitted to the Municipality for its approval taking specific cognisance of visual impact given the size and scale of the agricultural buildings and facilities and their location in a rural landscape, and in their proximity to tourist routes.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>agri-village</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> agri-village means a private settlement of restricted size established and managed by a legal institution that is situated within an agricultural area and where residence is restricted to bona fide agri-workers and their dependents of the farms involved in the development. Security of tenure does not include freehold but can include a Trust, Communal Property Association or Sectional Title. The development of agri-villages represents a partnership between farmer, agri-worker and state.</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_11" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_11"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_11__item_a" Municipality constitutes the development parameters.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_11__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_11__item_c"><span street, open space, railway line or a public street, open space, railway line or any other land utilised for transport purposes.</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_12" characteristics are sufficient to ensure safe and efficient operation of the street, road or parking.</span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>airfield</b></span><span to every site, use and type of building.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>backpackers lodge</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> backpackers lodge means a building where lodging for applicable to guest lodge apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>bed and breakfast establishment</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_18" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_18"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b> Land use description:</b> bed and breakfast establishment means a dwelling house, second dwelling or additional dwelling unit</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_18__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_18__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">in which the owner of the dwelling supplies lodging and meals for compensation to transient guests who have permanent residence elsewhere; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_18__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_18__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">provided that the dominant use, structure and design of the dwelling house concerned remains for the living accommodation of a single family.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to dwelling house, second dwelling and additional dwelling unit apply.</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_19" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_19"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following further parameters apply:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_19__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_19__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">no more than two rooms per land unit may be used for bedroom accommodation for paying guests, and no more than four paying guests per land unit may be supplied with lodging or meals at any time;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_19__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_19__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the requirement in paragraph (a) is also applicable where a land unit contains both a bed and breakfast establishment and rooms which are available for letting to lodgers;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_19__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_19__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the owner of a bed and breakfast establishment must live on the property and inform the Municipality in writing before the establishment opens for business;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_19__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_19__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">any new structure or alteration to the property related to its use as a bed and breakfast establishment must be compatible with the residential character of the area, particularly with regard to the streetscape or rural character on a farm, and must be capable of reverting to use as part of the dwelling house, second dwelling, additional dwelling unit or outbuilding concerned;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_19__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_19__item_e"><span consumption on the premises with meals;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_19__item_g" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_19__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span in the dwelling;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_19__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_19__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">no signage, and the size of the sign may not exceed 1 m in area;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_19__item_j" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_19__item_j"><span use.</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_20" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_20"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-item" with the site development plan that has been approved by the Municipality.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_20__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_20__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">Floor factor</span><span class="akn-p">The maximum floor factor is 2.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_20__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_20__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The highest point of a building may not exceed 10 metres to the top of the roof.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_20__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_20__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_20__item_d__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Building lines</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_20__item_d__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_20__item_d__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The street building line is at least 10 metres.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_20__item_d__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_20__item_d__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">Side and rear building lines are 0 metres or at least 10 metres if the site abuts any single residential zone or general residential zone.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_20__item_d__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_20__item_d__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">The general building line encroachments in this by-law apply.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_20__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_20__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">Parking, access and loading</span><span class="akn-p">Parking and access must be provided on the land unit in accordance with this by-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_20__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_20__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">Refuse room</span></span></span><span class="akn-p">A refuse room must be provided on the land unit in accordance with this by-law.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>boarding house</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_21" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_21"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> boarding house means a building where lodging is provided, and includes ancillary communal cooking, dining and other communal facilities for the use of lodgers, together with such outbuildings as are normally used in connection with a boarding house; and</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_21__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_21__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">includes a building in which rooms are rented for residential purposes, a guest house or guest lodge, a home for the aged, a residential facility for handicapped persons or orphans; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_21__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_21__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include a hotel, dwelling house, second dwelling, backpackers lodge or group house.</span></span></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">Coverage</span><span class="akn-p">The maximum coverage is 60%.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">Floor factor</span><span class="akn-p">The floor factor may not exceed 1.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_c__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">*Height</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The highest point of a building may not exceed 15 metres to the top of the roof.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">The general provisions regarding earth banks and retaining structures in this by-law apply.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_d__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_d__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Building lines</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_d__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_d__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The street building line is at least 5 metres.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_d__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_d__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">Side and rear building lines are at least 4,5 metres.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_d__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_d__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">The general building line encroachments in this by-law apply.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">Parking and access</span><span class="akn-p">Parking and access must be provided in accordance with this by-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">Screening</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may require screening in accordance with this by-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_g" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">Site development plan</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may require a site development plan to be submitted for its approval.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_h" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_h__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_h__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Open space</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_h__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_h__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Every boarding house must have access to an outdoor living area on the land unit, which may include private, or communal open space, but             excludes roads, service yards and parking areas.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_h__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_h__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">An outdoor living area of at least 10% of the net erf area must be provided.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_h__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_h__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">Such outdoor living area(s) must be of reasonable proportions and location, to the satisfaction of the Municipality, to allow for leisure or recreational use by residents, and may include open courtyards within the complex.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Service yard</span><span class="akn-p">A service yard must be provided on the land unit in accordance with this by-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_22__item_j" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_22__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">Refuse room</span><span class="akn-p">A refuse room must be provided on the land unit in accordance with this by-law.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>builders yard</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_23" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_23"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> builders yard means a property used for the storage of material and equipment which</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_23__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_23__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">is required for or is normally used for construction work;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_23__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_23__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">was obtained from demolitions of structures or excavations of ground; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_23__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_23__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">is necessary for, or is normally used for land development, such as storage of material used for building roads, installing essential services, or for any other construction work, whether for public or private purposes.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to industry apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>business premises</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_24" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_24"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> business premises means a property from which business is conducted and</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_24__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_24__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">includes a shop, big box retail, supermarket, restaurant, sale of alcoholic beverages, two electronic or mechanical playing devices, plant nursery, office, funeral parlour, financial institution and building for similar uses, place of assembly, institution, hotel, hospital, conference facility, rooftop base telecommunication station and multiple parking garage;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_24__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_24__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_24__item_b__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_24__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">includes also the following land uses above ground floor only:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_24__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_24__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">flats,</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_24__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_24__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">caretakers quarters,</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_24__item_b__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_24__item_b__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">backpackers lodge,</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_24__item_b__list_1__item_iv" and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_24__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_24__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include a place of entertainment, motor repair garage, industry, noxious trade, risk activity, adult entertainment, adult services or adult shop.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following development parameters apply:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">Coverage</span><span class="akn-p">The maximum coverage for all buildings on a land unit is 100%.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">Street centre line setback</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may require a street centre line setback, in which case all buildings or structures on a land unit must be set back at least 8 metres from the centre line of the abutting public street or streets.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">Floor factor</span><span class="akn-p">The maximum floor factor on the land unit is 3, which may be departed from if subsection(h) is complied with.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_d__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_d__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Height</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_d__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_d__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The highest point of a building may not exceed 15 metres to the top of the roof.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_d__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_d__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">The general provisions regarding earth banks and retaining structures in this by-law apply.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_e__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_e__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Building line</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_e__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_e__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The street building line is 0 metres.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_e__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_e__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">Side and rear building lines are 0 metres, provided that the Municipality may lay down common building lines in the interest of public health and safety or in order to enforce any other law or right.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_e__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_e__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">Minor architectural and sunscreen features may project beyond the street boundary building line, provided that such features do not project more than 250 millimetres beyond the street boundary.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">Hotel floor space concession</span><span class="akn-p">Where it is proposed to erect a hotel of at least 30 bedrooms in terms of this use right, the development parameters applicable to hotel apply.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_g" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">Canopy or balcony projection</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_g__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_g__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The Municipality may require, and may approve, a canopy or balcony projection over the street boundary in accordance with the following conditions:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_g__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_g__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the canopy or balcony may not project closer than 500 millimetres to a vertical plane through the kerb line or proposed kerb line;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_g__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_g__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">no portion of a canopy or balcony projection may be less than 2,8 metres above the pavement;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_g__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_g__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">the Municipality may lay down more restrictive requirements relating to the dimensions, design and materials of the canopy or balcony; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_g__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_g__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">the owner must enter into an encroachment agreement with the Municipality and register a servitude area in the case of a balcony projection.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_h" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">Public pedestrian footway along street boundary</span><span class="akn-p">If the owner provides a public pedestrian footway of at least 3 metres wide on the land unit, next to a building situated alongside the street boundary, with a canopy and pavement that ties in with the street pavement, and which is accessible to the public at all times, then, in recognition of the urban design contribution to the street environment, the maximum floor space of the building may be increased by twice the area of the public pedestrian footway.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Street corners</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may require that the owner of a building which is to be situated at a public street corner, and which the Municipality considers to be significant, must incorporate in the building architectural features which focus visual interest on the corner, and which emphasise the importance of pedestrian movement around the corner. Such features may include building cut-offs, walkthrough covered arcades, plazas or other elements.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_j" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_j__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_j__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Parking and access</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_j__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_j__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Parking and access must be provided on a land unit in accordance with this by-law, except in a case where the Municipality has approved alternative parking supply under subsection 42.(1).</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_j__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_j__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">Except with the approval of the Municipality, no parking bays at ground floor level on a land unit, either outside or within a building, may be located closer than 10 metres to a street boundary in order to enhance amenity at street level.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_k" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">Loading</span><span class="akn-p">Loading bays must be provided on the land unit in accordance with this by-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_l" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_l"><span class="akn-num">(l)</span><span class="akn-p">Screening</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may require screening in accordance with this by-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_25__item_m" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_25__item_m"><span class="akn-num">(m)</span><span class="akn-p">Refuse room</span><span class="akn-p">A refuse room must be provided on the land unit in accordance with this by-law.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>camping site</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> camping site means land set aside for camping where tents or caravans are used for accommodation of guests and which may include facilities for use of such visitors and features amenities such as facilities for outdoor food preparation, a small convenience store, road access for vehicles, picnic facilities, raised platforms on which to set up tents or caravans, ablution facilities, communal scullery and laundry facilities and waste disposal facilities.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to tourist accommodation apply provided that a site development plan must be submitted to the Municipality for its approval.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>caretakers quarters</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> caretakers quarters means an outbuilding of not more than 60 m in total floor area, including sanitary and cooking facilities, which is used for the accommodation of a caretaker employed at an industrial site or business premises where the operation requires that somebody is on the land unit at all hours.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">As determined by the Municipality.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>cemetery</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_26" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_26"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b> Land use description:</b> cemetery means a place for the burial of human or domestic animal remains, and</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_26__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_26__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_26__item_a__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_26__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">includes</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_26__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_26__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">ancillary buildings such as an office and chapel;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_26__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_26__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">a garden of remembrance or a wall of remembrance; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_26__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_26__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include a crematorium.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to public open space apply in the case of publicly owned land, and the parameters applicable to private open space apply in the case of land in private ownership.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>clinic</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_27" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_27"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> clinic means a place for the diagnosis and treatment of human illness or the improvement of human health, which has limited facilities and an emphasis on outpatients, provided that</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_27__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_27__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a clinic may contain live-in facilities for no more than 20 persons, including patients and staff; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_27__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_27__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a clinic may include medical consulting rooms, operating theatres, an outpatients centre, and a wellness centre with ancillary uses.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to place of instruction apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>conference facility</b></span><span class="akn-p">Land use description: conference facility means a place where information is presented and ideas or information exchanged among groups of people or delegates, and includes the supply of meals to delegates, as well as a function venue.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to business premises apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>container site</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> container site means property used for the storage of shipping or transport containers.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to industry apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>convenience shop</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> convenience shop means a small retail concern that is open long hours and that typically stocks a range of everyday items such as groceries, snack foods, candy, toiletries, soft drinks, tobacco products, newspapers and magazines.</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_28" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_28"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_28__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_28__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to service station apply.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_28__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_28__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">When approved as a consent use in another zone, the development parameters applicable to shop apply.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>correctional facility</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> correctional facility means a place where persons are housed and trained on instruction of a court of law and includes a reformatory, place of detention; industrial school and prison.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to authority use apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>crche</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> crche means the use of a building or the portion of a dwelling house or outbuildings by the occupant to provide day care, pre-school, play group or after-school care services for children.</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_29" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_29"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_29__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_29__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">The services provided must primarily be day care and educational, and not medical services.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_29__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_29__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">The services may not operate outside the hours 6:00 to 18:00.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_29__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_29__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">The dominant use of the dwelling house must remain for the living accommodation of a single family.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_29__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_29__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">Not more than 20 children may be registered at a time, or on the property at any time.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_29__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_29__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">Parking and access must be provided in accordance with this by-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_29__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_29__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">Registration with the Department of Social Services is compulsory.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>crematorium</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_30" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_30"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b> Land use description:</b> crematorium means a place for incinerating corpses in a furnace, and includes</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_30__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_30__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">ancillary facilities such as a chapel and offices; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_30__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_30__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a garden of remembrance or a wall of remembrance.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to industry apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>double dwelling house</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_31" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_31"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> double dwelling house means</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_31__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_31__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a building designed as a single architectural entity that appears as a single dwelling house, containing two dwelling units on one land unit; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_31__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_31__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span each of the two units may not exceed 250 m per unit.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_32__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_32__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_32__item_b__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_32__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Height</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_32__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_32__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The height of a double dwelling house may not exceed 6 metres from the base to the wall plate in all cases, and 8,5 metres to the ridge of the roof in the case of a pitched roof.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_32__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_32__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_32__item_d__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_cc" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_32__item_d__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_cc"><span class="akn-num">(cc)</span><span class="akn-p">exceed a width of 6,5 metres.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_32__item_d__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_32__item_d__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">A garage or carport may be erected within the street boundary building line if, in the opinion of the Municipality, compliance with the street boundary building line is not practical due to steep slopes of the ground between the road and the property concerned. The Municipality must determine the street boundary building line in such a case.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_32__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_32__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">Parking and access</span><span class="akn-p">Parking and access must be provided in accordance with the site access and parking layout requirements of this by-law, both dwelling units must     obtain vehicle access from and to a street, and at least one garage per dwelling unit must be provided for parking purposes, limited to a maximum     of two garages per dwelling unit.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_32__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_32__item_f"><span unit(s) concerned, in accordance with this by-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_32__item_g" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_32__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">Connection</span><span class="akn-p">The two units must be connected by means of a communal wall of the dwelling, and connected garages, outside lapas and braai areas may not be used to satisfy this requirement.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>dwelling house</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_33" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_33"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> dwelling house means a building containing only one dwelling unit, together with such outbuildings as
