by-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_34__item_e__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_34__item_e__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">Where a dwelling unit is occupied by unrelated persons as defined in (b) in the definition of family, provision must be made for parking in accordance with the parking requirements for a boarding house.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_34__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_34__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">Garaging</span><span class="akn-p">Garaging for up to four vehicles is permitted.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>environmental facilities</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> environmental facilities means facilities for the management, study, interpretation, education, and public appreciation of a predominantly natural area or heritage site and may include hiking trails, but does not include tourist facilities or tourist accommodation.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality must determine the land use restrictions and the development parameters for the property based on the objectives of this zoning and the specific circumstances including adherence with an approved environmental management plan, where applicable.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>factory</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> factory means property used for the assembly and manufacture of goods.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to industry apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>factory shop</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> factory shop means property used for the retail sale of goods that are completely or predominantly manufactured in a factory on the property concerned and may include a shop.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to industry apply.</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_35" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_35"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The occupant of an industry may operate a factory shop provided that</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_35__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_35__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the total floor space devoted to the sale of goods may not exceed 10% of the total floor space of all the buildings on the land unit; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_35__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_35__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">any goods that are offered for sale but have not been manufactured on the property, must be directly connected with the goods that are manufactured on the property.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>farm shop</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> farm shop means a building or structure located on a farm, which does not exceed 100 m in floor space, including storage facilities, where the farmer sells produce grown on the farm and other goods to the general public.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to agriculture apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>farmers market</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_36" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_36"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b> Land use description:</b> farmers' market means a predominantly fresh food market where farmers and food producers can sell farm-origin and associated value-added specialty foods and plant products directly to consumers which </span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_36__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_36__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">operates regularly within a community;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_36__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_36__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">is located at a focal public location that provides a suitable environment for farmers to conduct trade;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_36__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_36__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">typically consists of booths, tables or stands, outdoors or indoors, where farmers sell farm produce, meats, and sometimes prepared foods and beverages; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_36__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_36__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_36__item_d__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_36__item_d__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">includes </span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_36__item_d__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_36__item_d__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">primary food products;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_36__item_d__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_36__item_d__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">seafood, game and foraged foods;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_36__item_d__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_36__item_d__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">value-added foods;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_36__item_d__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_36__item_d__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">speciality food products;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_36__item_d__list_1__item_v" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_36__item_d__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">garden inputs; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_36__item_d__list_1__item_vi" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_36__item_d__list_1__item_vi"><span class="akn-num">(vi)</span><span class="akn-p">small livestock;</span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_37" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_37"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">and may include:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_37__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_37__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a subservient component of stalls for the sale of locally produced handmade crafts and arts;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_37__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_37__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">live family entertainment, outdoor recreation activities and childrens play area.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to agriculture, apply.</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_38" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_38"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following further parameters apply:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_38__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_38__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may stipulate conditions with regard to the layout, building design, open space, landscaping, parking, access and environmental management;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_38__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_38__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">The development may only occur in accordance with an approved site development plan.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>flats</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> flats means a building containing three or more dwelling units of which at least one does not have a ground floor, together with such outbuildings, open space and private roads as are ordinarily associated with flats.</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">Coverage</span><span class="akn-p">The maximum coverage is 60%.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">Floor factor</span><span class="akn-p">The floor factor may not exceed 1.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_c__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Height</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The highest point of a building may not exceed 15 metres to the top of the roof.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">The general provisions regarding earth banks and retaining structures in this by-law apply.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_d__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_d__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Building lines</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_d__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_d__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The street building line is at least 5 metres.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_d__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_d__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">Side and rear building lines are at least 4,5 metres.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_d__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_d__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">The general building line encroachments in this by-law apply.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">Parking and access</span><span class="akn-p">Parking and access must be provided in accordance with this by-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">Screening</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may require screening in accordance with this by-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_g" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">Site development plan</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may require a site development plan to be submitted for its approval.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_h" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">Institution, place of instruction and place of assembly</span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters that apply to institution, place of instruction and place of assembly apply to this use; provided that where the institution, place of instruction or place of assembly is situated within a building which is also used for flats or a boarding house, then the coverage, height and building line requirements for the flats or boarding house apply.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_i__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_i__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Open space</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_i__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_i__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Every block of flats must have access to an outdoor living area on the land unit, which may include private, or communal open space, but excludes roads, service yards and parking area.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_i__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_i__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">A outdoor living area of at least 10% of the net erf area must be provided; such outdoor living area(s) must be of reasonable proportions and location to allow for leisure or recreational use by residents, and may include open courtyards within the complex.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_j" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">Service yard</span><span class="akn-p">A service yard must be provided on the land unit in accordance with this by-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_k" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">Refuse room</span><span class="akn-p">A refuse room must be provided on the land unit in accordance with this by-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_l" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_l"><span class="akn-num">(l)</span><span class="akn-p">Flats as a consent use in a group housing scheme</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_l__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_l__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following conditions apply to flats as a consent use right in this zone:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_l__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_l__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the flats must form an integrated part of a group housing site and must comply with the development parameters for group housing;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_l__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_l__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the total floor space of flats may not exceed 40% of the total floor space of all buildings on the group housing site; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_39__item_l__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_39__item_l__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">the open space requirement for dwelling units in a group housing site applies.</span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>freestanding base telecommunication station</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> freestanding base telecommunication station means a freestanding support structure on land or anchored to land and used for telecommunication infrastructure to transmit or receive electronic communication signals, and may include any access roads to such facility.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to utility service apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>function venue</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> function venue means a building or structure used for functions, weddings, conference facilities and expos on what is mainly a rural property.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to agriculture apply on a rural property, together with the limitation that any function venue in a rural area may not exceed a total floor space of 500 m, which includes all components of the venue.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>funeral parlour</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_40" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_40"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description</b>: funeral parlour means property where the dead are prepared for burial or cremation and</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_40__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_40__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">includes facilities for ancillary administrative and religious functions; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_40__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_40__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include a crematorium.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to shop and industry apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>garden of remembrance</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> garden of remembrance is a section of a cemetery or crematorium set aside for the erection of memorial plaques or structures, placing or scattering of ashes.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to cemetery and crematorium apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>group housing</b></span><span class="akn-p">Land use description: group housing and group housing scheme means a group of separate or linked dwelling units where every dwelling unit has a ground floor, which units may be cadastrally subdivided but are planned, designed and built as a harmonious architectural entity in an ordered way and integrated with communal private open spaces, private roads and parking.</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b> Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">Design principles</span><span class="akn-p">All buildings and structures must be planned, designed and built as a harmonious architectural entity and special attention must be given to aesthetics, architectural coordination, urban design and landscaping.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">Density</span><span class="akn-p">The maximum gross density on a group housing site is 35 dwelling units per hectare.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_c__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Height</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The height of dwelling units may not exceed 6 metres from the base to the wall plate in all cases, and 8,5 metres to the ridge of the roof in the case of a pitched roof.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">The general provisions regarding earth banks and retaining structures in this by-law apply.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">Open space</span><span class="akn-p">Within a group housing site, outdoor space of at least 50 m per dwelling unit must be provided, which may include private or communal open space or any functional outdoor space which is inaccessible to motor vehicles, but excludes roads, service yards and parking areas.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">Building lines along the perimeter of a group housing site</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_e__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_e__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following building lines apply along the perimeter of a group housing site:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_e__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_e__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">a street boundary building line of 5 metres applies where the group housing site abuts an external public street;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_e__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_e__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">side and rear boundary building lines are 3 metres along the perimeter of the group housing site; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_e__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_e__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">the general building line encroachments in this By-law apply.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">Building lines within a group housing site</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_f__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_f__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following building lines apply within a group housing site:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_f__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_f__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">street boundary building lines on internal roads are 0 metres; provided that any garage door facing the road must be set back at least 5 metres from the kerb of such internal road; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_f__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_f__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">side and rear boundary building lines within the group housing site are 0 metres, unless the Municipality requires a building line for fire-fighting purposes, in which case the common boundary building lines must be determined by the Municipality.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_g" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_g__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_g__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Parking and access</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_g__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_g__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Parking and access must be provided in accordance with the requirements of this By-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_g__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_g__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">Parking may be provided in the form of communal parking.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_h" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">Site development plan</span><span class="akn-p">A site development plan of the proposed group housing scheme must be submitted to the Municipality for its approval, and, if approved, the development of the group housing site must be substantially in accordance with the approved site development plan.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Service yard</span><span class="akn-p">Service yard(s) must be provided on the land unit in accordance with this by-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_41__item_j" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_41__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">Refuse room</span><span class="akn-p">A refuse room must be provided on the land unit in accordance with this by-law.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>guest house</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_42" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_42"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> guest house means a dwelling house, second dwelling or additional dwelling unit which is used for the purpose of supplying lodging and meals to transient guests for compensation, in an establishment which exceeds the restrictions of a bed and breakfast establishment (more than 2 guest rooms or 4 guests), and</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_42__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_42__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">includes business parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to dwelling house, second dwelling and additional dwelling unit apply.</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_43" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_43"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following further parameters apply:</span><span class="akn-item" submitted for a proposed guest house and the guest house may not open for business until such plan is approved;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_43__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_43__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the owner of a proposed guest house must live on the property;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_43__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_43__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">any new structure or alteration to the property related to its use as a guest house must be compatible with the residential character of the area, particularly with regard to the streetscape, and must be capable of reverting to use as part of the dwelling house, second dwelling, additional dwelling unit or outbuilding concerned;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_43__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_43__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">no more than 6 rooms per land unit may be used for bedroom accommodation for paying guests or lodgers, and no more than 12 paying guests or lodgers may be supplied with lodging or meals at any time;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_43__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_43__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_43__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_43__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">no alcoholic beverages may be sold except to resident guests for consumption on the premises with meals;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_43__item_g" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_43__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">meals may only be supplied to guests or lodgers who have lodging on the property, employees, and the family residing in the dwelling;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_43__item_h" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_43__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">no advertising sign may be displayed other than a single un-illuminated sign or notice not projecting over a public street in accordance with the Municipalitys policy or By-law on outdoor advertising and signage, and the sign may not exceed 1 m in area;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_43__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_43__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">no activities may be carried out which constitute, or are likely to constitute, a source of public nuisance;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_43__item_j" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_43__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">on-site parking must be provided in accordance with the provisions of this By-law, provided that the Municipality may at any stage require additional on-site parking if, in the opinion of the Municipality, the guest house does not have enough parking; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_43__item_k" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_43__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">Registration with the local Tourism Board is compulsory.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>guest lodge</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_44" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_44"><span from 8:00 to 13:00 on Saturday. No home child care services are permitted on public holidays or Sundays.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_49__item_h" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_49__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">Areas for indoor play space and outdoor play space must be provided in accordance with any health requirement or a policy plan as might be approved by the Municipality from time to time, and outdoor play space must be fenced off from any public street or neighbouring property by a 1,8 metre-high fence or wall.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_49__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_49__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">No advertising sign may be displayed, other than a single un-illuminated sign or notice, not projecting over a public street, and the sign may not exceed 1 m in area.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_49__item_j" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_49__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">At least one off-street parking bay must be provided, plus one additional parking bay which is suitable for drop off and collect their children, unless the Municipalitys approval is obtained to waive this requirement. The Municipality may at any stage require additional on-site parking where, in the opinion of the Municipality, the home child care service does not have enough parking for its operations.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_49__item_k" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_49__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">Registration with the Department of Social Services is compulsory.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>home for the aged</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_50" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_50"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Land use description: home for the aged means a building where permanent lodging is provided, with or without meals, to persons who are 50 years of age or older and </span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_50__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_50__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_50__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_50__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">such data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_50__item_a__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">frail care facility;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_50__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_50__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_50__item_b__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_50__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">does not include </span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_50__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_50__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">hotel;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_50__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_50__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">bed and breakfast establishment; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_50__item_b__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_50__item_b__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">flats.</span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to boarding house, apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>home occupation</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> home occupation means the practising of an occupation or the conducting of an enterprise by one or more occupants who reside on the property, provided that the dominant use of the property concerned must remain for the living accommodation of the occupants and home occupation does not include a house shop.</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_51" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_51"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Development parameters</b></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_51__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_51__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">The dominant use of the property must be for accommodation of a single family.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_51__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_51__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">The proprietor of the home occupation concerned must live on the property.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_51__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_51__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">Any new structure or alteration to the property to accommodate a home occupation must be compatible with the residential character of the area, particularly with regard to the streetscape, and must be capable of reverting to use as part of the dwelling house, second dwelling or outbuilding concerned.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_51__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_51__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">Not more than three employees may be engaged by the occupant in the home occupation concerned.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_51__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_51__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">No home occupation may include a noxious trade, risk activity, adult entertainment, adult services, adult shop, sale of alcoholic beverages, motor repair garage, funeral parlour or activities that are likely to generate a public nuisance, including but not limited to panel beating and spray painting, auto electrician, builders yard, welding works or joinery.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_51__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_51__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">No goods for sale may be publicly displayed and no external evidence of the home occupation may be visible from a public street, except for an advertising sign in accordance with paragraph (g).</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_51__item_g" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_51__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">No advertising sign may be displayed other than a single, un-illuminated sign or notice not projecting over a public street in accordance with the Municipalitys outdoor advertising and signage By-law, and the sign may not exceed 0,2 m in area.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_51__item_h" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_51__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">No activities may be carried out which constitute or are likely to constitute a source of public nuisance, or generate waste material which may be harmful to the area or which requires special waste removal processes.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_51__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_51__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Off-street parking must be provided at a ratio of 1 parking bay per 25 m area used for home occupation. The Municipality may at any stage require additional on-site parking where, in the opinion of the Municipality, there is not enough parking for the home occupation concerned.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_51__item_j" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_51__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">The total area used for all home occupation activity on a land unit, including storage, may not consist of more than 25% of the total floor area of the dwelling units on the land unit or 50 m, whichever is smaller.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_51__item_k" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_51__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">The storage of all goods and equipment connected with the home occupation concerned must be inside a building or screened from neighbours and the public street.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_51__item_l" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_51__item_l"><span class="akn-num">(l)</span><span class="akn-p">Not more than two vehicles may be used in connection with a home occupation, and no one vehicle may exceed 3 500 kg in gross weight.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_51__item_m" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_51__item_m"><span class="akn-num">(m)</span><span class="akn-p">The hours of operation of a home occupation may not extend beyond 8:00 to 17:30 from Monday to Friday, and 8:00 to 13:00 on Saturday. No home occupation operations are permitted on public holidays or Sundays.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_51__item_n" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_51__item_n"><span class="akn-num">(n)</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may, at any stage, call for a cessation of the home occupation activity or impose conditions in order to minimise any potential nuisance to surrounding neighbours or the general public.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_51__item_o" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_51__item_o"><span class="akn-num">(o)</span><span class="akn-p">When home occupation is approved as a consent use right in any zone, the development parameters of home occupation apply over and above the development parameters of the relevant land use allowed as a primary right in the zone.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_51__item_p" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_51__item_p"><span class="akn-num">(p)</span><span class="akn-p">In order to exercise the consent use right under paragraph (o), the owner must obtain the written consent, where applicable, of the relevant owners association or Body Corporate, or all the owners within a housing scheme if the owners association or Body Corporate is not functioning.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>hospital</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_52" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_52"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> not specifically referred to in paragraph (a)(i) to (vii) must also be included in the floor space calculation of the building.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>house shop</b></span><span the property; provided that the dominant use of the property must remain for the living accommodation of the occupants and that the area occupied by the house shop retail trade does not exceed 25% of data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Floor factor and coverage</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_57__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The floor factor may not exceed 1,5.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_57__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">The maximum coverage is 75%.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_57__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_57__item_b__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Height</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_57__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The highest point of a building may not exceed 15 metres from the base to the top of the roof.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_57__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">The highest point of a stack of shipping or transport containers stored outside a building may not exceed 15 metres above average ground level.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_57__item_b__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_b__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">The general provisions regarding earth banks and retaining structures in this By-law apply.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_57__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">Street boundary building line</span><span class="akn-p">The street boundary building line is 0 metres, with a street centreline setback of at least 8 metres.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_57__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">Side and rear boundary building lines</span><span class="akn-p">Side and rear boundary building lines are 0 metres, provided that the Municipality may lay down side and rear building lines of up to 3 metres in the interest of public health and/or safety.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_57__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">Boundary walls</span><span class="akn-p">Where a land unit has a common boundary with another land unit that is not zoned Industrial Zone II or Industrial Zone III, the Municipality may require a 1,8 metre-high wall to be erected, to the satisfaction of the Municipality, along the common boundary.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_57__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">Parking and access</span><span class="akn-p">Parking and access must be provided on the land unit in accordance with this By-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_57__item_g" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">Loading</span><span class="akn-p">Loading bays must be provided on the land unit in accordance with this By-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_57__item_h" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">Screening</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may require screening in accordance with this By-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_57__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Hazardous substances</span><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the fact that an activity constitutes a primary use right in terms of this zone, no activity or use which includes the on-site storage of hazardous substances may be permitted unless a risk management and prevention plan has been submitted to the Municipality for its approval. Such a risk management and prevention plan must include guidelines approved by the Municipality to prevent or minimise danger to the environment or humans from a particular activity or series of activities, and to deal with the consequences of any dangerous event involving such hazardous substances.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_57__item_j" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">Industrial hive</span><span class="akn-p">The same development management provisions which apply to an industrial hive under light industry apply to an industrial hive in this zone.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_57__item_k" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">Site development plan</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may require a site development plan to be submitted for its approval in accordance with this By-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_57__item_l" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_57__item_l"><span class="akn-num">(l)</span><span class="akn-p">Refuse room</span><span class="akn-p">A refuse room must be provided on the land unit in accordance with this By-law.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>informal trading</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> informal trading means the legal selling of products in areas demarcated by the Municipality specifically for these purposes, including markets and other areas demarcated in accordance with the Municipalitys informal trading By-law.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">As determined by the Municipality.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>institution</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_58" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_58"><span the aged, retired, indigent or handicapped;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_58__item_a__list_1__item_iv" facility.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to place of instruction apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>intensive animal farming</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_59" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_59"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use wildlife.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to agriculture apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>intensive horticulture</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_60" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_60"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use otherwise;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_61__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_61__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">involves data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">Floor factor</span><span class="akn-p">The maximum floor factor on the land unit is 1,5.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">Coverage</span><span class="akn-p">The maximum coverage for all buildings on a land unit is 75%.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_c__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Height</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">No building may exceed a height of 8,5 m.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">The general provisions regarding earth banks and retaining structures in this By-law apply.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">Street building line</span><span class="akn-p">The street building line is at least 5 metres.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">Side building line</span><span class="akn-p">The side building line is at least 3 metres.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">Rear building line</span><span class="akn-p">The rear building line is at least 3 metres.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_g" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">Boundary walls</span><span class="akn-p">Where a land unit has a common boundary with another land unit which is not zoned for industrial purposes, the Municipality may require a 1.8 metre-high wall to be erected to the satisfaction of the Municipality along the common boundary.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_h" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">Parking and access</span><span class="akn-p">Parking and access must be provided in accordance with this By-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Loading bays</span><span class="akn-p">Loading bays must be provided in accordance with this By-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_j" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">Screening</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may require screening in accordance with this By-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_k" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">Refuse room</span><span class="akn-p">A refuse room must be provided on the land unit in accordance with this By-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_l" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_l"><span class="akn-num">(l)</span><span class="akn-p">Hazardous substances</span><span class="akn-p">No activity which includes storage of on-site hazardous substances may be permitted unless a risk management and prevention plan has been submitted to the Municipality for its approval. Such a risk management and prevention plan must include guidelines approved by the Municipality to prevent or minimise danger to the environment or humans from a particular activity or series of activities, and to deal with the consequences of any dangerous event involving such hazardous substances.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_m" Municipality for its approval.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_n" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_n"><span class="akn-num">(n)</span><span class="akn-p">Industrial hive</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_n__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_n__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following additional development parameters apply for an industrial hive, namely:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_n__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_n__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the design principles which are reflected in the definition of industrial hivemust be closely followed and implemented;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_n__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_n__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">special attention must be given to aesthetics, architectural coordination, urban design and landscaping; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_62__item_n__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_62__item_n__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">the Municipality may impose conditions specifying limits on the mix of retail and manufacturing activities, and the industrial hive may not allocate more than 50% of the total floor space to retail activities, shops or associated uses.</span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>liquor store</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> liquor store means an establishment where the dominant use is the retail sale of alcoholic beverages, for the consumption off the property.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to shop apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>medical consulting rooms</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> medical consulting rooms means an office or offices and ancillary rooms used by a registered medical professional for human medical or medical-related consultation, where such office is not attached to a hospital or clinic.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to office apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>mine</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> mine means mine as defined in the Mineral and Petroleum Resources Development Act, 2002 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/2002/28" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/2002/28">Act 28 of 2002</a>) and includes extracting gas for market production purposes.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_63" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_63"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following development management provisions apply:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_63__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_63__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">The owner must comply with national and provincial statutory requirements applicable to mining.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any application to rezone land to Industrial Zone IV must contain an explanation of the measures that will be implemented to address safety and environmental concerns which may be imposed as conditions of approval by the Municipality, including but not limited to:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">control of drainage, sedimentation and erosion;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">preservation of surface and substance water;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">preservation of topsoil;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">provision for restoration and the re-use of the site;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b__list_1__item_v" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">provision for noise and visual buffering;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b__list_1__item_vi" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b__list_1__item_vi"><span class="akn-num">(vi)</span><span class="akn-p">accommodation of heavy traffic and vehicles on roadways; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b__list_1__item_vii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_63__item_b__list_1__item_vii"><span class="akn-num">(vii)</span><span class="akn-p">a phased programme for rehabilitation.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_63__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_63__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">A site development plan must be submitted to the Municipality for its approval.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>mobile home</b></span><span class="akn-p">Land use description: mobile home means a transportable structure which is designed so that it can be used as a permanent dwelling and which has the necessary service connections for a permanent dwelling.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">As determined by the Municipality.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>motor repair garage</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> motor repair garage means a commercial enterprise where motor vehicles are provided with fuel or major services including engine overhauling, spray-painting, panel beating, black-smithery, exhaust fitment, shock absorber fitment or body work, and includes a service station.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_64" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_64"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The development parameters applicable to shop apply. The following additional development parameters apply:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_64__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_64__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">A site development plan must be submitted to the Municipality for its approval.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_64__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_64__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">Any part of the property of a motor repair garage which is used for the repair of motor vehicles, the storage of inoperable motor vehicles or parts of motor vehicles, empty containers such as oil drums and packing cases, or any other scrap, must be enclosed with a solid screen wall at least 2 metres high, or contained in a building.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any motor repair garage that supplies fuel must comply with the following access requirements:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the width of motor vehicle carriageway crossings over the street boundary, whether one-way or two-way, may not exceed 8 metres;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">a wall, at least 100 millimetres thick and 350 millimetres high, must be erected on the street boundary between different motor vehicle carriageway crossings, and such a wall must continue along such boundary unless the property is otherwise enclosed;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">the motor vehicle carriageway crossings must be limited to two per site unless the total length of a street boundary exceeds 30 metres, in which case one additional motor vehicle carriageway crossing may be permitted;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_iv__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_iv__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">at the point where it crosses the street boundary, a motor vehicle carriageway crossing may not be closer than:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_iv__list_1__item_aa" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_iv__list_1__item_aa"><span class="akn-num">(aa)</span><span class="akn-p">30 metres to the intersection of a provincial road and with any other road of a similar status;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_iv__list_1__item_bb" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_iv__list_1__item_bb"><span class="akn-num">(bb)</span><span class="akn-p">30 metres to the nearest point of an intersection where traffic is controlled, or is proposed to be controlled, by a traffic signal or traffic island;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_iv__list_1__item_cc" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_iv__list_1__item_cc"><span class="akn-num">(cc)</span><span class="akn-p">10 metres from the corner of an intersection not described in items (aa) and (bb), if such intersection is not splayed, or 5 metres from the point where the splay meets the road boundary if such intersection is splayed; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_iv__list_1__item_dd" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_iv__list_1__item_dd"><span class="akn-num">(dd)</span><span class="akn-p">1,5 metres from a side boundary; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_v" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_64__item_c__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">no fuel pump shall be erected so that the base or island on which the pump stands is less than 3,5 metres from the nearest street boundary.</span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>multiple parking garage</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> multiple parking garage means a place, excluding a road, street and on-site parking associated with a primary or consent use, that is used for parking of motor vehicles by the public, with or without a fee, and may include parking within a building.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to business premises apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>nature conservation area</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> nature conservation area means the use and management of land with the objective of preserving the natural biophysical characteristics of that land, such as the fauna and flora, but does not include tourist facilities, tourist accommodation or agriculture.</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_65" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_65"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b> Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-item" position of all structures, services and internal roads.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>nature reserve</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_66" for fauna and flora in their natural habitat that</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_66__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_66__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span exceed a height of 15metres.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_70__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_70__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span is at least 5 metres.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_70__item_d__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_70__item_d__list_1__item_ii"><span must be provided on the land unit in accordance with this By-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_70__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_70__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">Boundary walls</span><span class="akn-p">Where a land unit has a common boundary with another land unit that is not zoned Industrial Zone II or Industrial Zone III, the Municipality may require a 1,8 metre-high wall to be erected along the common boundary, of which the quality and finishing must be to the satisfaction of the Municipality.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_70__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_70__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Hazardous substances</span><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the fact that an activity constitutes a primary use right in terms of this zone, no activity or use which includes the on-site storage of hazardous substances is permitted unless a risk management and prevention plan has been submitted to the Municipality for its approval. Such a risk management and prevention plan must include guidelines approved by the Municipality to prevent or minimise danger to the environment or humans from a particular activity or series of activities, and to deal with the consequences of any dangerous event involving such hazardous substances.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_70__item_j" class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">Floor factor</span><span class="akn-p">The floor factor may not exceed 1.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_74__item_b" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_74__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_74__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">Street centre line setback</span><span class="akn-p">The municipality may require that all buildings or structures on the land unit are set back at least 6,5 metres from the centre line of the abutting street or streets.</span></span><span class="akn-item" The site development plan as approved constitutes the development parameters for such private parking.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>private road</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_83" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_83"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> private road means privately owned land which provides vehicle access to a separate cadastral property or properties and which is designated as private road; and</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_83__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_83__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">includes utility services and ancillary access control infrastructure, including a gatehouse, guardhouse, refuse room and utility room; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_83__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_83__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include a driveway on a property, or a servitude right of way over a property as these do not constitute private roads for the purpose of this zoning scheme.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">As determined by the Municipality.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>prospecting</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> prospecting means the first stage of physical search for minerals, fossils, precious metals or mineral specimens and may be granted as a temporary departure from this By-law by the Municipality since it does not constitute a primary, consent or occasional use right in terms of this By-law.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">As determined by the Municipality.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>public open space</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> public open space means land which is designated as public open space, under the ownership of the Municipality or other public authority, and which is not leased nor will be leased on a long-term basis, with or without access control, and which is set aside for the public as an open space for recreation or outdoor sport, including a park; playground; public or urban square; picnic area; public garden; nature area; and includes ancillary buildings and infrastructure.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_84" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_84"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following development parameters apply:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_84__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_84__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality must require a site development plan to be submitted for its approval.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_84__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_84__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">The site development plan as approved by the Municipality constitutes the development parameters for a primary use, if applicable, and a consent use.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>public parking</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> public parking means property that is accessible to the general public for parking purposes with or without a fee and/or access control.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">A site development plan must be submitted to the Municipality for its approval. The site development plan as approved constitutes the development parameters for such private parking.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>public street</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_85" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_85"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> public street means any land indicated on an approved plan, diagram or map as having been set aside as a public thorough way for vehicles and pedestrians, of which ownership as such vests in the Municipality; and includes </span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_85__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_85__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">open public parking areas;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_85__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_85__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">sidewalks;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_85__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_85__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">those parts of a public place that are travelled parts;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_85__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_85__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">informal trading ; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_85__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_85__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">appropriate and necessary street furniture and infrastructure, including reticulation networks, which does not present any threat to the safety or obstruct or inhibit free movement of pedestrians.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">A site development plan must be submitted to the Municipality for its approval. The site development plan as approved constitutes the development parameters for such public street.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>quarry</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> quarry means a place from which dimension stone, rock, construction aggregate, riprap, sand gravel or slate is excavated from the ground. A quarry is a type of open-pit mine that produces building materials and dimension stone.</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_86" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_86"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_86__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_86__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to agriculture together with additional parameters determined by the Municipality apply.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_86__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_86__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">If a quarry is approved as a consent use in Agricultural Zone I, the consent may only be granted for the number of years equal to the expected lifetime of the quarry concerned.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_86__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_86__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">The owner must comply with national and provincial statutory requirements applicable to mining.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any application to rezone land to Industrial Zone IV must contain an explanation of the measures that will be implemented to address safety and environmental concerns which may be imposed as conditions of approval by the Municipality, including but not limited to:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">control of drainage, sedimentation and erosion;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">preservation of surface and substance water;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">preservation of topsoil;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">provision for restoration and the re-use of the site;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d__list_1__item_v" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">provision for noise and visual buffering;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d__list_1__item_vi" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d__list_1__item_vi"><span class="akn-num">(vi)</span><span class="akn-p">accommodation of heavy traffic and vehicles on roadways; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d__list_1__item_vii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_86__item_d__list_1__item_vii"><span class="akn-num">(vii)</span><span class="akn-p">a phased programme for rehabilitation.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_86__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_86__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">A site development plan must be submitted to the Municipality for its approval.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>rehabilitation centre</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> rehabilitation centre means a facility providing treatment for substance abuse.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to place of instruction apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>renewable energy structure</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> renewable energy structure means any wind turbine, solar energy generating apparatus (including solar photo-voltaic and concentrated solar thermal), hydro turbines or bio mass facility or any grouping thereof, that captures and converts wind, solar radiation or bio mass into energy for commercial and includes any appurtenant structure necessary for, or directly associated with, generation of renewable energy, or any test facility or structure which may lead to the generation of energy on a commercial basis, excluding the electrical grid connections.</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_a__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Height</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The maximum height of a renewable energy structure is technology dependent.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">The height of buildings may not exceed 8,5 metres from natural ground level to the top of the roof.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item"
