id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">Setback</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_b__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">In the case of a wind turbine, the setback is a distance equal to 1,5 times the overall height of the turbine, measured from the average ground level to the highest blade tip, and then the setback is measured from-</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the nearest residential, commercial or critical agricultural structures such as animal housing, outbuildings, store rooms, excluding structures such as water troughs, feed dispensers, and windmills;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">a distance of 100m from the cadastral boundary of the land unit, unless the renewable energy structure straddles two or more cadastral boundaries, in which setback related to the straddled cadastral boundaries does not apply;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_b__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_b__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">a distance of 100m from any public road or private or public right of way, unless it provides access to the turbine;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_b__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_b__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">a distance of 100m from any electrical infrastructure; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_b__list_1__item_v" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_b__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">a distance of 1000m from towns, settlements or urban areas.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_c__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Site development plan</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">A site development plan must be submitted to the Municipality for its approval.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">The site must be surveyed and the exact delineation of the construction footprint must be shown in the site development plan.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_c__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_c__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">To the extent necessary, any relevant measures contained in these regulations must be incorporated into the site development plan submitted to the Municipality for approval.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">Visual and environmental impact</span><span class="akn-p">Negative visual and environmental impacts must be minimised to the satisfaction of the Municipality.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_e__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_e__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Land clearing, soil erosion and habitat impact</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_e__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_e__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The clearing of natural vegetation is limited to that which is necessary for the construction, operation and maintenance of the renewable energy structure as regulated by applicable environmental legislation.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_e__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_e__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">Wind turbines, solar structures, access roads and other infrastructure must be located to minimise damage to natural vegetation, water courses and wetlands.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_e__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_e__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">All land cleared which does not form part of the footprint of a renewable energy structure must be rehabilitated according to a rehabilitation plan for the land concerned, approved by the Municipality.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_e__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_e__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">Constructing or operating the renewable energy structure may not cause soil erosion, and any high-risk erosion areas must be rehabilitated by the operator, to the satisfaction of the Municipality.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_e__list_1__item_v" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_e__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">The applicant must prove, to the satisfaction of the Municipality, that planning for the renewable energy structure concerned has taken into account and mitigated the risk of all impacts in respect of, and necessary distances which should be maintained from, wetlands, water bodies, threatened ecosystems, mountains, ridges, hills, coastal buffers, settlements, telecommunication towers, transmission towers and power lines.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_e__list_1__item_vi" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_e__list_1__item_vi"><span class="akn-num">(vi)</span><span class="akn-p">The applicant must provide exact coordinates relevant to land clearing, soil erosion and habitat impact to assist the Municipality to evaluate the risk of possible negative environmental impacts of the renewable energy structure concerned.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">Noise, air quality and nuisance</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_f__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_f__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The development must be compliant with regulations controlling pollution, including</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_f__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_f__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the National Environmental Management Act, 1998 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1998/107" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1998/107">Act 107 of 1998</a>);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_f__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_f__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">provincial regulations in force; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_f__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_f__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">Municipal By-laws.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_g" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_g__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_g__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Finishing, colour and design</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_g__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_g__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">A wind turbine structure must be treated with a neutral, non-reflective exterior colour designed to blend in with the surrounding natural environment, to the satisfaction of the Municipality.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_g__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_g__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">A solar structure must minimise any adverse effects related to its reflective surfaces and must be designed and built in a way that mitigates this impact, as required by the Municipality.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_h" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_h__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_h__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Appurtenant structures</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_h__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_h__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">All appurtenant structures to a renewable energy structure prescribed by the Municipality concerning bulk, height, yard sizes, building lines, open space, parking and building coverage requirements are subject to applicable By-laws.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_h__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_h__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">Appurtenant structures, including, but not limited to, equipment shelters, storage facilities, transformers and sub-stations must be architecturally compatible with the receiving environment as required by the Municipality, and contained within a renewable energy structure site development plan submitted for approval by the Municipality.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_h__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_h__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">Appurtenant structures may only be used for the storage of equipment or other uses directly related to the operation of the particular facility with which they are associated.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_h__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_h__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">Appurtenant structures must be screened from view by indigenous vegetation and/or located in an underground vault, or be joined and clustered to minimise adverse visual impacts.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_i__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_i__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Lighting</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_i__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_i__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">A renewable energy structure or any part of such a structure may only be lit for safety and operational purposes and the lighting must be appropriately screened from abutting land units.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_i__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_i__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">A renewable energy structure must comply with the lighting air safety requirements of the South African Civil Aviation Authority in terms of the Civil Aviation Act, 2009 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/2009/13" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/2009/13">Act 13 of 2009</a>).</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_j" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">Signage and advertising</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_j__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_j__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Signs on renewable energy structures must comply with national and local signage regulations and be limited to signage necessary to</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_j__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_j__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">identify the operator;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_j__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_j__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">provide 24-hour emergency contact numbers; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_j__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_j__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">provide warning of any dangers associated with the structure.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p">No commercial advertising, including advertising for the provider or operator, may be displayed on any renewable energy structure.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_k" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">Maintenance</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_k__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_k__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The owner is responsible for maintaining a renewable energy structure in good condition, including any access road, unless deemed a public way, and for paying the cost of repairing any damage resulting from construction or operation. Maintenance must include, but is not limited to</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_k__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_k__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">painting;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_k__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_k__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">structural repairs;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_k__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_k__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">rehabilitation measures; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_k__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_k__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">the upkeep of security and safety measures.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_l" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_l"><span class="akn-num">(l)</span><span class="akn-p">Modification</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_l__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_l__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any modification to a renewable energy structure, excluding inconsequential in situ technical improvements, made after approval and which is not in accordance with the approval and its conditions, requires authorisation from the Municipality within the parameters of these regulations by means of</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_l__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_l__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the amendment of approved conditions;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_l__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_l__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">a new consent use approval;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_l__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_l__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">amendment of the approved site development plan; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_l__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_l__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">amendment of the approved building plan.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m"><span class="akn-num">(m)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Decommissioning</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Any renewable energy structure and associated infrastructure which has reached the end of its productive life or has been abandoned, including buildings, cables and roads, must be removed by the owner.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">A renewable energy structure is considered abandoned when the structure fails to continuously operate for more than two years.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">When a renewable energy structure is scheduled to be decommissioned or operations have been discontinued or it has been abandoned, the land owner must, by registered mail, notify the Municipality within 30 days after the operation ceased, and of plans for removal of the structure and infrastructure referred to in subparagraph (i).</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">The owner is responsible for the removal of the structure in all its parts, within 150 days after the date of discontinued operation, or as agreed upon by the Municipality after submission of a plan for decommissioning. The Municipality may, for reasons which are justifiable in its opinion, grant an extension of the deadline for removing the structure and its parts. The land must then be rehabilitated, to the satisfaction of the Municipality, to the condition prescribed in the approved environmental management plan and the approved decommissioning plan.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_v" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_v__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_v__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Decommissioning must include, inter alia</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_v__list_1__item_aa" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_v__list_1__item_aa"><span class="akn-num">(aa)</span><span class="akn-p">the removal of all renewable energy structures and appurtenant structures, including equipment, bases, foundations, security barriers and transmission lines directly related with the renewable energy.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_v__list_1__item_bb" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_v__list_1__item_bb"><span class="akn-num">(bb)</span><span class="akn-p">disposal of all solid and hazardous waste in accordance with provincial and local waste disposal regulations; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_v__list_1__item_cc" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_v__list_1__item_cc"><span class="akn-num">(cc)</span><span class="akn-p">the stabilisation and re-vegetation of the site with indigenous vegetation to minimise erosion.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_vi" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_vi"><span class="akn-num">(vi)</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may, in order to minimise erosion and disruption to natural vegetation and habitats, grant permission to the owner to depart from the decommissioning plan in respect of removing landscaping, underground foundations or other underground components, provided these do not cause any pollution.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_vii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_vii"><span class="akn-num">(vii)</span><span class="akn-p">Prior to the construction of the renewable energy structure commences, the owner must make financial provision or an alternative reasonable arrangement, to the satisfaction of the Municipality, for protection against failure at any time after site construction has started for the rehabilitation or management of negative environmental impact of decommissioning or of abandonment in the event of the owner being unable to fulfil necessary financial obligations.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_viii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_viii"><span class="akn-num">(viii)</span><span class="akn-p">If the owner fails to remove the structure or its parts in accordance with the requirements of these regulations within 150 days of abandonment or the date of decommissioning or an approved extension date, the Municipality may enter the property and remove the structure and its parts, and to recover all removal costs incurred from the owner.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_ix" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_m__list_1__item_ix"><span class="akn-num">(ix)</span><span class="akn-p">If the owner fails to meet the requirements of subparagraph (i) the Municipality may after written notice to the owner, use all or part of the financial provision or other provision referred to in subparagraph (vii) to rehabilitate or manage the negative environmental impact or to remove the facility.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_87__item_n" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_87__item_n"><span class="akn-num">(n)</span><span class="akn-p">Urban Areas</span><span class="akn-p">No renewable energy structure shall be permitted within an urban area, other than solar voltaic energy generating apparatus.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>resort shop</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> resort shop means a shop that provides for the daily needs of the inhabitants of a holiday resort which may include a retirement resort.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The floor space of a resort shop may not exceed 100 m.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>restaurant</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> restaurant means a commercial establishment where meals and liquid refreshments are prepared or served or prepared and served to paying customers primarily for consumption on the property, and may include licensed provision of alcoholic beverages for consumption on the property, and the option for customers to purchase food for consumption off the property.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters as applicable to business premises apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>retirement resort</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_88" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_88"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> retirement resort means flats, group housing or town housing that conforms to the following additional conditions:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_88__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_88__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">each dwelling unit must be occupied by a retiree or pensioner or by a family of which at least one member is a retiree or pensioner; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_88__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_88__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a full spectrum of frail care and other facilities reasonably associated with a retirement resort may be provided at such a retirement resort.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters of the applicable general residential zones apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>riding school</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> riding school means a place or undertaking for the leasing of horses and riding instructions against payment, and includes the care and stabling of the horses.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters of the applicable agricultural zone apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>risk activity</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> risk activity means an undertaking where the material handled or the process carried out is liable to cause extremely rapid combustion, give rise to poisonous fumes, or cause explosion, and includes major hazardous installations and activities involving dangerous and hazardous substances that are controlled in terms of national legislation.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to noxious trade apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>rooftop base telecommunication station</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> rooftop base telecommunication station means a support structure attached to the roof, side or any part of a building and used to accommodate telecommunication infrastructure for the transmitting or receiving of electronic communication signals.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">The general provisions of section 31 of this By-law apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>scrap yard</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_89" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_89"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> scrap yard means a property which is utilised for one or more of the following purposes:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_89__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_89__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">storing, depositing or collecting of junk or scrap material or articles the value of which depend mainly or entirely on the material used during their manufacture;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_89__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_89__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the dismantling of second-hand vehicles or machines to recover components or material; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_89__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_89__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the storage or sale of second-hand parts, poles, steel, wire, lumber yards, tyres, bricks, containers or other articles which are suited to being left in the open.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to industry apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>second dwelling</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> second dwelling means another dwelling unit which may, in terms of this By-law, be erected on a land unit where a dwelling house is also permitted; and such second dwelling may be a separate structure or attached to an outbuilding or may be contained in the same structure as the dwelling house; provided that the second dwelling must remain on the same land unit as the dwelling house and not be alienated separately.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_90" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_90"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The development parameters applicable to dwelling house apply, together with the following additional parameters:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_90__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_90__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">The total floor space of a second dwelling unit may not exceed 150 m, which includes the floor space of all ancillary buildings.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_90__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_90__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">A second dwelling must be constructed in a style that does not detract from the architecture of the main dwelling house.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_90__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_90__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">A second dwelling that is a separate structure to a dwelling house may not exceed a height of 6 metres from the base to the top of the roof.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_90__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_90__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">A second dwelling may not be alienated by means of sectional title within any type of single residential zone.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_90__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_90__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">A second dwelling that is contained within the same building as a dwelling house must be designed so that the building appears to be a single dwelling house; both units may have a ground floor, or one unit may be on the ground floor and the other unit above.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_90__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_90__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">The existence of a second dwelling may not in itself be sufficient reason for the Municipality to grant an application in terms of planning law to subdivide the land unit containing the dwelling units.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_90__item_g" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_90__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">The construction of a second dwelling may be subject to the Municipalitys municipal services department certifying that adequate services network capacity is available to serve the needs of the second dwelling.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>service station</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_91" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_91"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> service station means property for the retail supply of fuel, and</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_91__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_91__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">include uses such as washing of vehicles, a convenience shop and a restaurant; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_91__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_91__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include spray-painting, panel beating, motor repair garage, open air motor vehicle display or truck stop.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_92" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_92"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The development parameters applicable to shop apply. The following additional development parameters apply:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_92__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_92__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">A site development plan must be submitted to the Municipality for its approval. The site development plan must at least address matters pertaining to vehicle access, risk management of fuel pumps and fuel storage areas, screening and minimising any visual intrusion or operational disturbance with adjoining properties.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_92__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_92__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_92__item_b__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_92__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any service station must comply with the following access requirement:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_92__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_92__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the width of motor vehicle carriageway crossings over the street boundary, whether one-way or two-way, may not exceed 8 metres.</span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>service trade</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_93" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_93"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> service trade means an enterprise which is</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_93__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_93__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">primarily involved in the rendering of a service for the local community including the repair of household appliances or the supply of household services;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_93__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_93__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">not likely to be a source of disturbance to surrounding properties;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_93__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_93__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">employs at most 10 people;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_93__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_93__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">not likely, in the event of fire, to cause extremely rapid combustion, give rise to poisonous fumes or cause explosions;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_93__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_93__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">includes laundry, bakery, dairy depot, and similar types of uses; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_93__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_93__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include an abattoir, brick-making site, builders yard, sewage works, service station, open air motor vehicle display or motor repair garage.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters</b></span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters applicable to shop apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>shelter</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_94" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_94"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Land use description: shelter means a unit of accommodation, intended for human occupation with such outbuildings as are ordinarily used with a dwelling unit, constructed of any material whatsoever, even though such material may not comply with the standards of durability intended by the National Building Regulations; and includes</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_94__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_94__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">residential purposes;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_94__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_94__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a storeroom;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_94__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_94__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">garaging;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_94__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_94__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">renewable energy structures for household purposes; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_94__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_94__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">home occupation.</span></span></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_95" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_95"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_95__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_95__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">It is the sole responsibility of the occupant or owner of the shelter to ensure the structural, habitability, fire resistance or other standards of a shelter.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_95__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_95__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may instruct any occupant or owner of a shelter to take action to remedy a public safety, health or fire risk.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_95__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_95__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">The dominant use of the unit must remain residential.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_95__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_95__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">No noxious trade, risk activity, adult entertainment, adult services or adult shop is permitted in a shelter.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_95__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_95__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">No activities may be carried out in a shelter which constitute or are likely to constitute a source of nuisance, including the use of equipment that generates excessive noise, or any activity which results in the generation of dust, fumes, smoke, or waste material which could be detrimental to health, or which requires special waste removal processes.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_95__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_95__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may, at any stage, call for a cessation of the land use or activity, or impose conditions in order to minimise any potential nuisance to surrounding neighbours or the general public.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_95__item_g" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_95__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">Coverage</span><span class="akn-p">There is no restriction on coverage.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_95__item_h" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_95__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">Height</span><span class="akn-p">A shelter structure may not exceed two storeys and its height is restricted to 8,5 metres from the base to the top of the shelter.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_95__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_95__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_95__item_i__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_95__item_i__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Building lines</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_95__item_i__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_95__item_i__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Side building lines are at least 1 metre on one side or 1,5 metres in the case where the shelter has windows or doors.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_95__item_i__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_95__item_i__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">If a midblock sewage system is present, a rear building line of up to 2 metres may be required by the Municipality.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_95__item_i__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_95__item_i__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">The street building line is 1 metre, if required by the Municipality.</span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>shop</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_96" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_96"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b> Land use description:</b> shop means property used for the retail sale of goods and services to the public, and</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_96__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_96__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">includes a retail concern where goods which are sold in such a concern are manufactured or repaired, a funeral parlour, service trade, clinic and the sale of motor vehicles; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_96__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_96__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include a hotel, industry, supermarket, motor repair garage, open air motor vehicle display, service station, adult entertainment business, adult services or adult shop.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following development parameters apply:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">Floor factor</span><span class="akn-p">The maximum floor factor on the land unit is 1.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">Coverage</span><span class="akn-p">The maximum coverage of all buildings on a land unit is 75%.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_c__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Height</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The maximum height of a building is 8,5 metres to the top of the roof.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">The general provisions regarding earth banks and retaining structures in this By-law apply.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">Street centreline setback</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may require a street centreline setback, in which case all buildings or structures on the land unit must be set back 8 metres from the centre line of the abutting public street or streets.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_e" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">Street boundary building line</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_e__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_e__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The street boundary building line is 0 metres, subject to the following conditions:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_e__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_e__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the street centreline setback restriction in subparagraph (d);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_e__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_e__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">minor architectural and sunscreen features may project beyond the street boundary building line provided that such features do not project more than 250 millimetres beyond the street boundary; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_e__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_e__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">for service stations, the street boundary building line is 5 metres subject to the general building line encroachments in this By-law.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_f" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">Side and rear boundary building lines</span><span class="akn-p">The side and rear boundary building lines are 0 metres.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_g" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">Canopy projection</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_g__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_g__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The Municipality may approve a canopy projection over the street boundary in accordance with the following conditions:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_g__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_g__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The canopy may not project nearer than 500 millimeters to a vertical plane through the kerb line or proposed kerb line.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_g__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_g__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">No portion of a canopy projection may be less than 2,8 metres above the pavement.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_g__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_g__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may lay down more restrictive requirements relating to the dimensions, design and materials of the canopy.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_g__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_g__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">The owner must enter into an encroachment agreement with the Municipality in the case of a canopy projection.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_h" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">Street corners</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may require that the owner of a building which is to be situated at a public street corner, and which the Municipality considers to be significant, must incorporate in the building architectural features which focus visual interest on the corner, and which emphasise the importance of pedestrian movement around the corner; and such features may include building cut-offs, walk-through covered arcades, plazas or other elements.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Parking and access</span><span class="akn-p">Parking and access must be provided on the land unit in accordance with this By-law, except in a case where the Municipality has approved alternative parking supply under subsection 42(1).</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_j" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">Loading</span><span class="akn-p">Loading bays must be provided on the land unit in accordance with this By-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_k" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">Screening</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may require screening in accordance with this By-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_l" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_l"><span class="akn-num">(l)</span><span class="akn-p">Repair or manufacturing concern in a shop</span><span class="akn-p">The floor space relating to any manufacturing or repair concern in a shop may not comprise more than 40% of the floor space of the shop.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_97__item_m" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_97__item_m"><span class="akn-num">(m)</span><span class="akn-p">Refuse room</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may require a refuse room to be provided on the land unit in accordance with this By-law.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>smallholding</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> smallholding means an extensive landholding of between 1 hectare and 5 hectares in extent on which small-scale agricultural activities may take place, but are primarily places of residence and include a dwelling house.</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_98" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_98"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_98__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_98__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to agriculture apply, except for building lines which are 10 metres from any boundary.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_98__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_98__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">Any newly created smallholding areas must be situated within the urban edge of a town.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>supermarket</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> supermarket means a shop having a total floor space larger than 400 m and up to 3000m, in which a range of goods, including foodstuff and household goods, is offered for sale on a predominantly self-service basis.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to shop apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>telecommunication infrastructure</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_99" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_99"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> telecommunication infrastructure means any part of the infrastructure of a telecommunication network for radio or wireless communication</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_99__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_99__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">including voice, data and video telecommunications, which may include antennae; and any support structure, equipment room, radio equipment or optical communications equipment (laser or infra-red) provided by cellular network operators and any other telecommunication provider; as well as all ancillary structures needed for the operation of telecommunication infrastructure; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_99__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_99__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include fibre optic installations and point-to-point copper (cable) installation and rooftop base telecommunication stations.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">As determined by the Municipality.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>tourist accommodation</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_100" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_100"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> tourist accommodation means a harmoniously designed and built holiday development, used for holiday or recreational purposes, whether in private or public ownership, that</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_100__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_100__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">consists of a single enterprise that provides overnight accommodation by means of short- term rental or time sharing only; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_100__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_100__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">may include the provision of a camping site, caravan park, chalets or mobile home park, and resort shop, private or public roads; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_101" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_101"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_101__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_101__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">The parameters of the existing lawful development apply as land use restrictions with regard to land which is deemed to be zoned as a resort zone with effect from the date of commencement of the Land Use Planning Act.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_101__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_101__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">When land is rezoned to Resort Zone I, the Municipality must lay down conditions with regard to density, layout, landscaping, and building design.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_101__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_101__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">A site development plan must be submitted to the Municipality for its approval, clearly indicating the position of all structures, stands, services and internal roads.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_101__item_d" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_101__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_101__item_d__list_1" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_101__item_d__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Provided that if a hotel or wellness centre is approved as a consent use within Resort Zone I, the following additional conditions apply:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_101__item_d__list_1__item_i" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_101__item_d__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Rooms may not be alienated by means of sectional title.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_101__item_d__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_101__item_d__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">The hotel or wellness centre may not accommodate more than 50% of the number of accommodation units.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_101__item_d__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_101__item_d__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">The architectural design of the hotel or wellness centre must conform to that of the rest of the resort.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_101__item_d__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_101__item_d__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">The maximum height for the hotel or wellness centre is 6 metres from the base to the wall plate in all cases and 8,5 metres to the top of the roof in the case of a pitched roof.</span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>tourist facilities</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_102" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_102"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Land use description: tourist facilities means amenities for tourists or visitors and</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_102__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_102__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">includes lecture rooms, restaurants, gift shops, restrooms, farmers market and recreational facilities; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_102__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_102__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include an off-road trail, a hotel, wellness centre; or tourist accommodation.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to agriculture apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>town housing</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> town housing means a row or group of linked or attached dwelling units, planned, designed and built as a harmonious architectural entity of which every dwelling unit has a ground floor and which dwelling units may be cadastrally subdivided.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_103" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_103"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The development parameters of group housing apply, provided that:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_103__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_103__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">Density</span><span class="akn-p">The maximum gross density on a town housing site is 60 dwelling units/hectare.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_103__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_103__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">Open space</span><span class="akn-p">The open space requirements for group housing do not apply to town housing.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_103__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_103__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">Coverage</span><span class="akn-p">The maximum coverage for all buildings on a land unit is 60%.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>transport use</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_104" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_104"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> transport use means the use of land, a building or structure for the operation of a service for the transportation of goods (including liquids and gases) or passengers by means of rail, road, sea or pipeline and</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_104__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_104__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">includes the use of that land, building or structure for the purpose of a harbour, railway station, bus depot or taxi interchange, and a transport undertaking; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_104__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_104__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">includes a public and/or private undertaking including a railway station, bus depot, multiple parking garage, taxi rank, public transport interchange, harbour and ancillary purposes; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_104__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_104__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include an airport, airfield; or helicopter landing pad.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to business premises apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>truck stop</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_105" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_105"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> truck stop means a facility with direct access from a freeway, inner city road or major transport route which</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_105__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_105__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">provides a range of rest, service and fuelling facilities for heavy duty, long haul vehicles and trucks, and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_105__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_105__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include accommodation.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_106" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_106"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Development parameters are determined by the Municipality by means of conditions of approval for a truck stop as a consent use, provided that</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_106__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_106__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the Municipality must require a site development plan to be submitted for its approval; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_106__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_106__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the site development plan must at least address matters pertaining to vehicle access, placement of overnight parking and ablution facilities/rest rooms, screening and minimising any visual intrusion or operational disturbance to adjoining properties.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>urban agriculture</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> urban agriculture means the cultivation of crops, on relatively small areas within the urban area or edge, for own consumption or sale in neighbouring markets; provided that cultivation of a garden by an occupant is not regarded as urban agriculture for the purpose of this zoning scheme.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">As determined by the Municipality.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>utility service</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_107" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_107"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> utility service means a use or infrastructure that is required to provide engineering and associated services for the proper functioning of urban development and</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_107__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_107__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">includes a water reservoir and purification works, electricity substation and transmission lines, storm water retention facilities, and a waste-water pump station and treatment works, rooftop base telecommunication station and freestanding base telecommunication station; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_107__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_107__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include renewable energy structures or transport use; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_107__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_107__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">provided that a road is not regarded as a utility service.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">As determined by the Municipality.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>wall of remembrance</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> wall of remembrance is a wall in a cemetery or crematorium section provided for the placement of inscribed tablets commemorating deceased persons.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to cemetery and crematorium apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>warehouse</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_108" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_108"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> warehouse means a building used primarily for the storage of goods, and-</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_108__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_108__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">includes property used for business of a predominantly wholesale nature, and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_108__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_108__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">does not include property used for business of a predominantly retail nature.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to industry apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>wellness centre</b></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_109" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_109"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><b>Land use description:</b> wellness centre means a business which provides a variety of services for the purpose of improving health, beauty and relaxation through personal care treatments such as massages, rehabilitation, exercise programmes, diet, instruction on wellness, life coaching, and facials which includes</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_109__item_a" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_109__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">facilities like saunas, pools, steam rooms, gymnasiums, treatment rooms, relaxation areas and whirlpools;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_109__item_b" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_109__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">accommodation where guests may reside; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_2/hcontainer_1__list_109__item_c" data-eId="hcontainer_1__list_109__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the provision of meals to guests.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to tourist accommodation apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>winery</b></span><span class="akn-p"><b>Land use description:</b> winery means a place where wine is made, and may include a selling point to the general public and wine-tasting area.</span><span class="akn-p"><b>Development parameters:</b></span><span class="akn-p">Development parameters applicable to agriculture apply in agricultural areas and industry apply in industrial areas.</span></span></span></span></span>
</div>
<div class="akn-attachment" id="att_3" data-eId="att_3">
<h2 class="akn-heading">Schedule 3</h2>
<h2 class="akn-subheading">Overlay zones approved in terms of section 16</h2>
<span class="akn-doc" data-name="schedule"><span class="akn-mainBody"><section class="akn-section" id="att_3/sec_1" data-eId="sec_1"><h3>1. Subdivisional area overlay zone</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="att_3/sec_1__subsec_1-1" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1-1"><span class="akn-num">1.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">General purpose of Subdivisional Area Overlay Zone</span><span class="akn-p"><i>The subdivisional area overlay (SAO) zoning designates land for future subdivision with development rights by providing development directives through specific conditions as approved in terms of this By-law. The SAO zoning confirms the principle of development and acceptance of future subdivision of land; but not the detailed layout, which will be determined when an actual application for subdivision is approved.</i></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_3/sec_1__subsec_1-2" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1-2"><span class="akn-num">1.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Use of the property</span><span class="akn-p">Land zoned as a subdivisional area may be subdivided as contemplated in the Municipal Planning By-law.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_3/sec_1__subsec_1-3" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1-3"><span class="akn-num">1.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Development parameters</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_3/sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">When the municipality approves a subdivisional area overlay zone, it must impose conditions making provision for at least</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">density requirements;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">main land uses and the extent of such uses; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_3/sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_c__list_1" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">a detailed phasing plan or a framework including</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">main transport routes;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">main land uses;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">bulk infrastructure;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">requirements of organs of state;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">public open space requirements; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_vi" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1-3__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_vi"><span class="akn-num">(vi)</span><span class="akn-p">physical development constraints.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="att_3/sec_2" data-eId="sec_2"><h3>2. Special planning overlay zone</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-1"><span class="akn-num">2.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">General purpose of special planning area overlay zone</span><span class="akn-p"><i>The general purpose of a package of plans is to provide for a mechanism to plan and manage the development of large or strategic urban development areas which also provides for a greater degree of flexibility. The package of plans mechanism is a phased process of negotiation, planning and approvals, where appropriate levels of planning detail are approved together with conditions for those approvals.</i></span><span class="akn-p"><i>A special planning area overlay zone is generally created in respect of an application which involves a mixed use development proposal or where the development does not generally comply with the development parameters of the applicable land uses of this zoning scheme.</i></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-2"><span class="akn-num">2.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-2__list_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Use of the property</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-2__list_1__item_2-2-1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-2__list_1__item_2-2-1"><span class="akn-num">2.2.1</span><span class="akn-p">Primary uses are as stipulated in the conditions of approval imposed in terms of the Municipal Planning By-law.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-2__list_1__item_2-2-2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-2__list_1__item_2-2-2"><span class="akn-num">2.2.2</span><span class="akn-p">Consent uses are as stipulated in the conditions of approval imposed in terms of the Municipal.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3"><span class="akn-num">2.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Development parameters</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-1"><span class="akn-num">2.3.1</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality must require a package of plans as set out in section 2.3.4 of Schedule 3 to be submitted for areas zoned as special planning area overlay zones.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-2"><span class="akn-num">2.3.2</span><span class="akn-p">The applicant must, during pre-application discussions with the Municipality, ascertain whether a package of plans procedure has to be followed.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-3" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-3"><span class="akn-num">2.3.3</span><span class="akn-p">The development parameters of the lowest order package of plans as contemplated in section 2.3.2 of Schedule 3 and as approved by the Municipality are the development parameters of the special planning overlay zone applicable to the property concerned.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4"><span class="akn-num">2.3.4</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The package of plans consists of the following components that are listed in a hierarchy from higher- order to lower-order plans, and the lower-order plans must be in compliance with the higher-order plan:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Contextual framework</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The contextual framework lays down broad land use policy for the development and the surrounding area.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">It may include principles or heads of agreement summarising the general obligations of the Municipality and the developer in relation to the development.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">The contextual framework may be prepared by the Municipality, or by a land owner or development agency under supervision of the Municipality, and may not be in conflict with a spatial development framework or structure plan approved by the Municipality.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Development framework</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">The development framework must identify overall policy, broad goals, and principles for development within the development.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">The development framework must identify the range of uses, general spatial distribution of uses, major transport and pedestrian linkages, infrastructure and any limits to development within the development, including but not limited to density and floor space.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_c__list_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Precinct plans</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"
