data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Precinct plans apply to specific areas within the development framework that have common features, functional relationships or phasing requirements.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">There may be several precinct plans that make up a development area.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">A precinct plan must describe in more detail the development objectives and intentions for a specific area in the development, as well as principles for urban form, land use, pedestrian links, traffic movement, floor space and environmental management.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_d__list_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_d__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Subdivision plans</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Subdivision plans, if required, must be processed in terms of planning law to establish new cadastral boundaries and to facilitate the transfer of land units.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">Subdivision plans may be approved at any stage after the development framework has been approved, and the provisions of section 15(2) apply to such plans.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_e__list_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_e__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Site development plans</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Site development plans depict more detailed design and development provisions for one or more land units within a development.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">These provisions may include (but are not limited to) details relating to land use, floor space, building lines, height, parking requirements, municipal services and landscaping, as well as details relating to the position and appearance of buildings, open space, pedestrian links and traffic movement.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">A site development plan may be required before or after a subdivision plan, and must provide for the information as required for a site development plan in terms of this By-law.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_f__list_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_f__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Building plans</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">Building plans contain detailed specifications as required by the National Building Regulations.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-4__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">Building work may only commence once building plans have been approved by the Municipality.</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-5" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-5"><span class="akn-num">2.3.5</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may require all or only some of the components of the package of plans to be applied in respect of a particular development.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-6" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-6"><span class="akn-num">2.3.6</span><span class="akn-p">The Municipality may require that the area covered by a contextual framework must extend beyond the land under consideration if, in its opinion, the proposed development will have a wider impact, and the Municipality may determine the extent of that area.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-7" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-7"><span class="akn-num">2.3.7</span><span class="akn-p">In approving a package of plans, the Municipality must determine the total floor space or density permitted within the development which must be imposed as a condition of approval.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-8" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-8"><span class="akn-num">2.3.8</span><span class="akn-p">The allocation of floor space must take into account the carrying capacity of internal and external infrastructure including roads and utility services, and any urban design principles approved by the Municipality as part of a rezoning or contextual framework.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-9" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-9"><span class="akn-num">2.3.9</span><span class="akn-p">The approved floor space may remain as floating floor space assigned to the overall development for later allocation, or may be assigned to particular precincts when a precinct plan is approved; and in either case must be allocated to individual subdivisions or site development plans.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-10" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-10"><span class="akn-num">2.3.10</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-10__list_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-10__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">When a special planning area overlay zone and a package of plans is required in terms of this zoning scheme, the relevant components must be submitted to the Municipality for its approval before any development on a land unit can commence, provided that</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-10__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-10__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the development may not be refused if it is consistent with the development parameters of a base zone, overlay zone, or condition of approval; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-10__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-10__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the Municipality may require amendments of detail to the site development plan to address reasonable concerns relating to access, parking, architectural form, urban form, landscaping, environmental management, engineering services or similar concerns.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_3/sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-11" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2-3__list_1__item_2-3-11"><span class="akn-num">2.3.11</span><span class="akn-p">The general provisions contained in this zoning scheme apply with regard to site development plans.</span></span></span></span></section></section></span></span>
</div></span></article></span>
